- I have heard that the **Most High** (*Tàishàng*), in His lofty exaltation, rules the **Three Heavens** (*Sāntiān*) with purity and distance, His universe vast, His **Sun and Moon** radiant, illuminating all things without exception. All malevolent ghosts are thus slain and annihilated.

If so, then:
- In the **East**, the **Green Plague** (*Qīngwēn*), **Green Toxin** (*Qīngdú*), and **Green Spasm** (*Qīngjìng*) arise, with the ghost named **High Reach** (*Gāoyuǎn*).
- In the **South**, the **Red Plague** (*Chìwēn*), **Red Toxin** (*Chìdú*), and **Red Sickness** (*Chìzhèng*) arise, with the ghost named **Scholar’s Speech** (*Shìyán*).
- In the **West**, the **White Plague** (*Báiwēn*), **White Toxin** (*Báidú*), and **White Sickness** (*Báizhèng*) arise, with the ghost named **White Fortune** (*Báixìng*).
- In the **North**, the **Black Plague** (*Hēiwēn*), **Black Toxin** (*Hēidú*), and **Black Epidemic** (*Hēizhòu*) arise, with the ghost named **Great Yellow Slave** (*Dàyuán núláo*), along with his seven sons, and male and female siblings, each propagating their own malevolent plague *qi*.

From the **First Month** to the **Twelfth Month**, each has its own plague ghosts, spreading freely and causing suffering throughout the land.

Moreover, in the **years of Jiazi, Yichou, Rényǐn, Mǎodǐng, Chénwèi, Sìwǔ, Wèiwǔ, Shēnshēn, Yǒuyǒu, Xǔyǒu, Hàiyǒu**, and the **Twelfth Month of Chén**, each plague ghost bears a name and rank.

From the **Twelve Earthly Branches** (*Shíèr shí*) of the day, the Five Directions, Five Colors, and the **Yellow Slave** (*Huángnúláo*)—the **Old Vermin** (*Lǎochóng*)—all descend upon us.

In this degenerate age, the foolish populace face calamities without end, dying in numbers beyond count.

Since the day I received the **Dao**, I have sworn to aid the nation and sustain life, to heal the people, and according to the **Scriptures of the Celestial Hierarchy** (*Kēwén*), to exterminate falsehoods and sweep away rebellious ghosts, all of which I have done.

Having been entrusted with this sacred office, I now humbly prostrate myself in petition, praying that the **Most High** (*Tàishàng*), the **Supreme Dao of the Limitless** (*Wújí Dàodào*), and all the **Honorable Lords** (*Zhūjūn zhàngrén*), may cover my household with Your boundless grace, utterly rooting out all malevolent spirits and eradicating their essence.

The **Celestial Officials** (*Shàngguān*)’s envoys shall, in due time, grant this decree.

I pray that:
- The **East**’s **Celestial Official** (*Qīngdì*) command **Victory** (*Chéng*) and **Absolute Cessation** (*Jué*) of the **Green Plague**,
- The **South**’s **Celestial Official** (*Chìdì*) command **Peace** (*Píng*) and **Absolute Cessation** (*Jué*) of the **Red Plague**,
- The **West**’s **Celestial Official** (*Báidì*) command **Exile** (*Qiān*) and **Absolute Cessation** (*Jué*) of the **White Plague**,
- The **North**’s **Celestial Official** (*Hēidì*) command **Lengthening** (*Cháng*) and **Absolute Cessation** (*Jué*) of the **Black Plague**,
- The **Central**’s **Five Father Lords** (*Wǔfùjūn*) command **Absolute Cessation** (*Jué*) of the **Yellow Plague** (*Huángwēn*).

For the **Four Cardinal Directions** (*Dōngxī nánběi*), the **Four Intermediate Directions** (*Sìwéi*), the **Twelve Branches of Time** (*Shíèr shí*), and all spirits within, may they all be commanded to guard against malevolence, preventing it from entering.

Furthermore, the **Celestial Sovereigns** (*Dì*) of the **East** (*Qīngdì*), **South** (*Chìdì*), **West** (*Báidì*), and **North** (*Hēidì*), in their singular power, shall simultaneously descend and bestow aid.

I earnestly appeal to the **King of Ten Thousand Ghosts** (*Bāi guǐ zhōngwáng*) of the **High Heavens** (*Gāotiān*), with **Twelve Thousand** (*Wàn èr qiān*) soldiers, each commanding **Eight Hundred Thousand** (*Bāi shíwàn*) troops, to join with the **subordinate officers** (*Shēnzhōng yìbīng*) within my person, as well as the **Three Generals** (*Sān jiāngjūn*) who guard this dwelling, the **Twenty-Four Officials** (*Èrshísì lì*), and the **Three Hundred Thousand** (*Sān bǎi shíwàn*) soldiers, all with blades in unison, encircling the dwelling in **three layers** (*Sāncéng*), and **two markets** (*Èr shì*) around the perimeter, their weapons pointing outward, to sweep away in one moment all malevolent, rebellious, and licentious spirits, utterly annihilating them.

The **Celestial Officials** (*Shàngguān*) shall, upon hearing my plea, reward my labor faithfully, without failing to fulfill my earnest trust.

I pray with deepest reverence.

**Petition for the Dissolution of Heavenly Nets and Earthly Snares** (*Jiě Tiānluó Dìwǎng Zhāng*), with proper ritual rank and position, states as follows:

*"My body and family suffer afflictions and calamities, fearing ensnarement by the Heavenly Nets and Earthly Snares. I have petitioned the officials, seeking this scroll for deliverance. Due to my limited learning, I do not grasp the **qi** and seasons, nor possess refined numerology. I rely solely on the **Six Jia** and **Five Phases** to determine cycles and fate.*

*By tradition, the **Steel-Hai** direction (absolute **yang**) is the **Heavenly Net**, while the **Chen-Si** direction (absolute **yin**) is the **Earthly Snare**. When one’s fate aligns with these, disaster follows. For men, if their **birth year** clashes with the **Tàisuì** (Yearly Official), their **birth month** becomes the **Heavenly Net’s transmission**, and their **conception month** the **Earthly Snare**. For women, if their **birth year** clashes with the **current year**, their **conception month** becomes the **Heavenly Net’s River Chief**, and their **birth month** the **Earthly Snare**. Additionally, if the **current year** clashes with their **birth year’s Tàisuì**, their **conception month** becomes the **Heavenly Net’s transmission**, and their **birth month** the **Earthly Snare**. Further, when the **Heavenly Halter** aligns with **Tàiyī**, it becomes the **Heavenly Net**. If the fetus resides in **Dēngmíng**, it becomes the **Earthly Halter**. Months of **Five Punishments, Six Calamities, Seven Injuries, and Nine Afflictions**, as well as years and months of decline, or when **Halter and Chief** clash in lethal combinations—these bring myriad disasters and misfortunes, causing untold harm.*

*I fear my household’s fate may collide with the **Five Directions’ Nets**, the **Nine Palaces and Eight Trigrams**, their mutual assaults, or the **Nine Heavens’ Primordial Qi** descending into the mortal realm, spanning **Nine Hundred and Ninety Li** in all directions. The **Net** burns like flames, the **Snare** looms like black clouds, both infused with the **Nine Stars’ essence**, their **Red Precision** blazing. If my fate aligns with these, ruin is immediate.*

*Now, I offer **ritual efficacy**—one bolt of undyed silk, **1,200 coins**, **12 dou of white rice**, **1.2 sheng of oil**, **120 sheets of paper**, **120 feet of red cord**, a pair of **handcuffs**, **1 liang of raw silk**, ink, brushes, incense, and lamps—humbly praying that the **Celestial Officials**, the **Most High’s Boundless Dao**, the **Heavenly Master’s Gate**, the **Five Qi Lords**, and the **Typists of Records** may deign to intervene:

- **East: Yín-Mǎo-Chén (Wood Qi Lords)**—dissolve the **East’s Green Affliction and Green Poison**.
- **South: Wù-Wǔ-Yǒu (Fire Qi Lords)**—dissolve the **South’s Red Affliction and Red Poison**.
- **West: Shēn-Yǒu-Xū (Metal Qi Lords)**—dissolve the **West’s White Affliction and White Poison**.
- **North: Hài-Zǐ-Chǒu (Water Qi Lords)**—dissolve the **North’s Black Affliction and Black Poison**.
- **Center: Wù-Jǐ (Earth Qi Lords)**—dissolve the **Center’s Yellow Affliction and Yellow Poison**.

*May the **Five Directions’ Qi** and the **Twelve Hours** pose no harm.*

*I have heard: the **upper three fives** belong to Heaven, the **middle three fives** to Man, the **lower three fives** to Earth. Heaven’s **Five Phases** govern clarity of sun and moon; Earth’s **Five Qi** nurture all things; Man’s **Five Constants** ensure vitality. When **ritual and music** are preserved, harmony is complete. I fear my household’s **Five Qi** are misaligned, my **zàng-fǔ** (viscera) disordered, the **Five Phases** clashing in destructive cycles. I humbly pray that the **Superior Officials** may:

- **Above**, dissolve the **Five Stars’ Auspicious Qi**,
- **Below**, lift the **Thirty-Six Earthly Taboos**,
- **Within**, absolve my **ten thousand sins and myriad offenses**.

*I further petition the **Seven Stars of the Big Dipper**:
- **Tānláng (Acquisition Wolf)** and **Jùmén (Supreme Gate)** to **sever the source of death**,
- **Lùcún (Luck Star)** and **Liánzhēn (Generosity)** to **replace the fatal form**,
- **Wénqū (Literary Curve)** and **Wǔqū (Martial Curve)** to **erase the death record**.

*I also petition the **Lords of Severing Afflictions, the Supreme Ancestral Blessing, the Lords of Fate and Qi, and the Jade Calendar Lords**, each with **120 officers**, to **apprehend and disperse my myriad calamities**, dissolving all afflictions—from the **First to the Ninth**—across my residence. May the **True Officials** record their **Qi**, oversee, and summon my **ancestors, parents, relatives, and in-laws**, granting them entry into the **Central Palace** for **official rank and rewards**, assigning them to bureaus by merit, promoting them by rank, and ensuring that the **living and the dead** receive blessings, with **spirits and mortals** aiding one another, so that my **lifespan may extend**, my **afflictions be surpassed**, and this petition proven true.*

*Humbly submitted to the **Most High’s Distinction*.*

「The *Dai Ma* (Relay Horse) Chapter also states the *Kai Du* (Opening the Way) Chapter:

*"[The following] rites and ranks are established. [I] humbly declare: I, by virtue of being born from the womb, and my descendants, have for a thousand years been fortunate enough to receive the blessings of the **Great Dao/Way** and to have always been under its grace. Now, in the year of the **Relay Horse** (驿马), which is a year of seeking blessings, if I do not submit a petition to **exhort and welcome** the **Relay Horse**, I fear there may be obstruction, harm to my lifespan, and stagnation in my official rank and stipends.

Yet, with only anxiety and no merit to cultivate, I rely solely on sincerity of heart to submit this petition, **appeasing and averting** the calamities of the **Relay Horse** and inviting the blessings of rank and stipends, so that no harm may come. Now, I present the **ritual oath** (法信), with a golden figure of a man, five-colored ceremonial offerings, and the aforementioned items, to establish my **sincere vow** (立心信) and seek to **remove and dispel** the calamities of the **Relay Horse**, to **ascend and bestow** wealth and stipends, to **transcend and escape** temporal disasters, and to **permanently ensure** the **Original Auspiciousness** (元吉), so that I may enter the **Diagram of Life** (生图) and exhort the **Relay Horse**, thereby preserving my lifespan. I pray that my entire household, great and small, may be spared from all other misfortunes.

I, as a humble subject, being ignorant and unversed in the **Dao/Way of Qi** (气候), have heard that the **Great Ease** (太易) has the **virtue/power** (功) of **rectifying faults and atoning for sins**, and that the **Retreating Armor** (遁甲) holds the **Dao/Way** of **seeking to establish and avoid calamities**.*

With utmost reverence, I petition the **August Heavenly Sovereign**, the **Royal and Ministerial Canopy**, the **North Pole Star Lord**, the **Three Celestial Lords of Fate and Fortune**, and the **Lord Who Supports Fate**, to uphold and exalt the **Relay Horse**, so that official rank and stipends may be fulfilled.

The **oil**, one *dou* and two *sheng*, is used to **illuminate the Void and Mysterious**.

The **black silk thread** and **divination tally**, to **prolong stipends and lifespan**. The **rice**, one *dan* and two *dou*, to **benefit the granaries**. The **paper, ink, and brush**, to **record and establish the Register of Life**. The **money**, one thousand two hundred *wen*, to **pledge the sincerity of the red heart**.

The **incense**, one *jin*, to pray that the **North Pole Star** removes one’s name from the **Register of Death** and the **South Pole Star** inscribes it in the **Register of Life**, thus extending lifespan endlessly.

I further petition the **Functionary Lords of Vital Qi**, to ascend to the **Supreme Mysterious Palace of Life**, requesting the **adjustment of stellar degrees and calculations**, to **replace and transform one’s name and form**.

I also petition the **Lord of Fate** and the **Lord Who Summons the Soul**, to proceed north to the **Dark Yin Lady of the Netherworld** and the **Lord Who Extends One’s Name**, each five in number, with **official attendants** numbering one hundred twenty, to **assist me in upholding and inviting the Relay Horse**, so that official rank and stipends may ascend in glory, while calamities and disasters are exterminated, and the **heart and viscera** shine with clarity. The **Eight Trigrams of Heaven and Earth—Kàn, Zhèn, Xùn, Lǐ, Kūn, and Duì—**, the **Twenty-Eight Lunar Mansions**, and the **Three Hills and Five Graves**, overseeing the **seasons and their nodes**, shall witness these meritorious deeds, cycling endlessly in their course.

I further petition the **General Who Protects Fate**, the **Lord of Ten Thousand Blessings**, the **Lord Who Relieves Affliction**, the **Lord of Qi Circulation**, and the **Lord Who Dissolves Calamities and Supports the Declining**, each fifteen in number, with **official attendants** numbering one hundred twenty, to **work in concert with me**, safeguarding my person and fate, elevating my official station, extending my years and augmenting my calculations, filling my granaries with grain and silk, and amassing wealth, thus **permanently preserving the Original Auspiciousness**.

The petitioned celestial officials, having accepted their roles, shall, according to the **Three Auspicious Days** of my petition, fulfill their functions without failing in their efficacy.

By the **Supreme Sage’s discernment**, pity my humble inadequacy.

Thus, through the **Two Official Direct Envoys**, the **Functionary of the Orthodox Unity**, the **Left and Right Official Envoys**, the **Divine Clerks of Yin-Yang**, the **Clerks of the Scarlet Talisman Carriage**, and the **Just Wind Cavalry Stationed at the Relay Horse**, each with two officials, I, **[Subject’s Name]**, humbly submit this **Petition for Harmonizing the Relay Horse, Removing Calamities, and Inviting Wealth and Stipends**, to be presented to the **[Relevant Bureau]**.

**Acknowledgment of the Five Tombs Petition**
With due observance of ritual rank, I humbly state:

According to the written records, **[Subject’s Name]**, of **[County]**, reports that in this **[month/day]**, **[his/her] illness** has worsened, with no improvement in recovery—fearing for **[his/her] life**. Since **[Subject’s Name’s]** three generations of ancestors and seven generations of forebears, their accumulated sins have invited calamities and retributions. Whether within the tombs, there are grievances and disputes, or the wrath of Heaven and Earth has caused the departed to rest uneasily, disturbing the living. Or perhaps the ancestral mounds have been severed, the cypress and pine felled by others, bricks dug from the tomb edges, or roads encroaching upon the burial grounds—deeply fearing that one day the spirits may sink into the depths of the underworld.

Having already petitioned the **Celestial Officials**, **Three Realms’ True Sovereigns**, and submitted the relevant documents, I now present this **Sacred Oath of the Dao** with offerings: one bolt of yellow silk, twelve *dou* of white rice, twelve *sheng* of oil, one thousand two hundred coins, paper, ink, incense, and fruit. I humbly pray to the **Supreme Dao** to accept this petition, absolve the departed, stabilize the tombs, and for both the living and the dead—through countless sins and transgressions—all may be cleansed.

I have also received oral instructions to present this petition to the **Celestial Bureau**, praying for Your **Merciful Inspection** and **Pardon** for all ancestors, both recently and long deceased, as well as for all past and present offenses, curses, grievances, and vengeful *qi* associated with the tombs. May all be severed, and may **[Subject’s Name]** recover swiftly, the departed rest in peace, and the tombs remain serene.

I further petition to **Acknowledge the Five Tomb Lords**, and also invoke the **Grand Star Marshal**, **Green Canopy Official Marshal**, **Supreme Clarity Palace Sovereign**, and the **Earthly Marshal**, each with one hundred twenty attendants, to descend and **Remove**[**Subject’s Name’s**] Illness and **Absolve the Departed**.

Whether the tomb lies at the **Dragon’s Head**, **Tail**, **Left**, **Right**, or **Foot**, or within the **Forbidden Zones of Movement and Coiling**, causing the spirits to tremble in terror and unrest, returning harm to the living—leading to **[Subject’s Name’s]** current **illness and afflictions**. I pray for the **Extinction of the Five-Tone Mound Officials**, the **Two-Thousand-Stone Tomb Guardians**, and all **Tomb *Qi* Officials**, so that the departed may rest undisturbed, free from calamities, and all offenses be pardoned.

May the living and the dead live without blame or punishment, all grievances resolved. May **[Subject’s Name’s]** household flourish, with unbroken lineage.

This shall not fail in its efficacy.

Your **Grace is Supreme**.

**To the Three Heavens’ Gate: Petition for Admission**

**Dissolving the Five Tombs’ Seal**

Your servant, **[Subject’s Name]**, of the **ranked position for petitioning laws**, humbly states:

In accordance with the **Mysterious Doctrine**, I now, by virtue of my native place **[Subject’s Native Region]**, kneel and submit myself. By nature, I was born of the womb, and my descendants are likewise born of the womb. Yet within my own person, this year marks the **Tomb Year**—the **Year of the Dog**—when I risk being ensnared by the **Five Tombs’ calamities** and the **Three Killings’ malevolence**.

Should a person enter the Tomb Year, they may be bound by the **Tomb God’s retribution**, ensnared by **ghostly qi**. Recently, my limbs have grown heavy, my appetite has waned, and I know not how to **redeem the Five Tombs’ disasters** or **sustain my life**. With sincere devotion, I appeal to the **Great Dao**, humbly beseeching Your discerning gaze, and earnestly pray for deliverance.

Now, I offer **faithful tokens**: five **substitute figures (锡人)**, one **stone and two dou of rice**, one thousand two hundred **copper coins**, one **bolt of plain cloth**, one **dou and two sheng of oil**, one hundred twenty **sheets of paper, writing brushes, and counting rods**, to petition for a **sealed decree** that severs the **deceased’s misfortunes**. May these **substitute figures** bear my form, **divert my calamities**, and **prolong my life**.

With reverence, I submit this **sealed petition** for Your celestial scrutiny.

I pray that the **Heavenly Tribunals’ officials** may extend mercy, inspect my case, and **grant absolution** for the **ten thousand sins and offenses** I have committed across seven lifetimes. May You further **cleanse and dispel** the **Five Tombs’ and Five Directions’ calamities**, substituting the **five figures** in my stead, so that my descendants may be spared from **erroneous suffering**.

I further petition for the **Returning-Life Lord, Longevity Lord, Prolonging-Life Lord, Extracting-Life Lord, Continuing-Life Lord, Supporting-Life Lord, and Augmenting-Life Lords**—five each—to be dispatched, along with one hundred twenty **official attendants**, to the **Southern Palace’s Bureau of Fate and Records**, to **redeem my life** for the **three cycles of the Three Treasures**, the **three hundred and one periods**, and to **dissolve the calamities** within my person.

May they **open the Celestial Gate**, **reverse my death registry**, and **transfer my name** to the **Green Ledger of Immortality**, securing my lineage for eternity.

After this petition, my lifespan shall be extended, the **Five Tombs’ retributions** severed, and their **disastrous punishments** transformed into **blessings**—thus proving the efficacy of this plea.

With gratitude to the **Supreme Primordial Worthies**, who distinguish truth from falsehood, I humbly seek but one moment of Your favor.

Thus, I append this petition in the same manner as before, only altering the **Direct Deity’s name**.

**For the Supplication of a Dying Person:**

In strict accordance with the prescribed rites, I humbly declare:

I have received the **Celestial Master’s** teachings, and now, according to my records, I kneel and submit this plea. Since birth, my descendants have been fortunate to receive the **Dao**, and I am truly delighted and at ease.

Yet, my faith has often strayed from the teachings, bringing misfortune and calamity upon me. Now, on the **certain day of the certain month**, I am gravely ill, my body burdened, and my dreams chaotic and unkind.

I sought divination, and it revealed that the **deceased** (*wángrén*) is causing harm, with repeated entanglements, leading to this unending illness. I fear that death will not cease, and the affliction will never end, filling my household with dread. I fear my life may not be spared.

Today, my heart is filled with earnest supplication, and I beg you for a cure. I have already composed this plea and submitted it to the **Heavenly Bureau**. I humbly await your decree.

The **Most High Venerable Lord Lao** (*Tàishàng Lǎojūn*), the **Most High Venerable Elder** (*Tàishàng Zhàngrén*), the **Heavenly Master Lord** (*Tiānshī Jūn*), and the **Master Beneath the Gate** (*Ménxià Zhǔ*)—may you grant me discernment.

I earnestly petition the **Lord of My Native Star** (*Běnmìng Jūn*) among the **Ten Myriad** (*Shíwàn*), that you may for me dispel the **entangling *qi*** (*fùlián zhī qì*) of the deceased who repeatedly harms me, and may it be severed.

The souls and spirits of the living belong to their **origin** (*shēngshǐ*), each **beginning** (*yīyuán yīshǐ*) distinct—separated by **ten myriads and ninety thousand** (*wànwàn jiǔshí yú lǐ*). The living owe allegiance to **Imperial Heaven** (*Huángtiān*), while the dead submit to **Yellow Springs** (*Huángquán*). Their paths diverge—let them not disturb my body.

Again, I fear that the deceased may have committed the **most heinous offense** (*mòdà zhī zuì*), or that in death they bear **unpardonable transgressions** (*bùshè zhī qiān*), confined within the **various prisons** (*zhūyù*). Sometimes they are in **River Lord’s Prison** (*Hébó zhī yù*), sometimes in **Lady Qing’s Prison** (*Nǚqīng zhī yù*), sometimes in the **City God’s Temple** (*Chénghuáng shèmiào*). I know not where the soul and shade of the deceased may dwell—pray, guide them to **transmigration** (*qiāndá*), that they may find peace, ascend to **Heaven’s Hall** (*Tiāntáng*), and enjoy **natural sustenance** (*yīshí zìrán*), wandering freely without care. May their **tombs and graves** (*fénmù ānwěn*) be secure, their **petitions and grievances** (*zhùsòng xiāochén*) laid to rest, and my illness within my body **immediately removed** (*jīméng chúyù*). May the entanglements cease and my wishes be fulfilled—this shall be proof of your efficacy.

With deepest gratitude to the **Most High Assembly of Worthies** (*Tàishàng Zhòngzhēn*).

**Translation:**

In strict accordance with the **Mysterious Ordinances**, it is now reported that [certain person] has long been unfaithful, inviting calamities and misfortunes. Recently, strange omens have multiplied, and illnesses have persisted, causing the entire household to live in dread. Through divination and calculations, it is revealed that the spirits of both ancestral and guest-deceased are resentful, tormenting the living. This is likely due to insufficient offerings during ancestral rites—insufficient food and drink at the seasonal sacrifices—inviting retribution from the vengeful dead.

Thus, we humbly beseech the **Supreme Daoist Lord of the Great Way** to guide and transmigrate these spirits, freeing them from suffering.

In addition, the undersigned petitions for the protection of **Five Guardian Lords** and **Five Protector Deities**, along with **one hundred twenty officials**, to oversee the exorcism of these malevolent spirits on behalf of [certain person]. May all illnesses and afflictions be pardoned and dispelled, confirming the efficacy of this plea.

With deepest gratitude to the **Most High Assembly of Worthies**.

How can this be averted?

**Petition for Mercy**

Your humble servant, on behalf of [name], respectfully submits a *Mouth Chapter* for the **Celestial Officials** to dispel the fire calamity, presented to the **Supreme Court of the [Specific] Palace of the Most High**.

The **Highest Clarity Merit Chapter** is duly registered in its proper rank. It is hereby declared that, upon reviewing the written petition, it is found that [name], a disciple of [specific state] and [specific county], aged [number], born in the [month] of [year], in deepest reflection, acknowledges his humble origins as one born of mere mortal flesh and blood. By fortune and fate, he has received the **Dao**, surrendered to the **True One**, and been nourished by the four seasons. The **Most High** cherishes life, abhors killing, and has bestowed upon this servant his *qi* and vital essence, extending even to this day. He has been graced by the **Enlightenment of the Sun**, and through the **Teacher’s Way**, has been granted the **Sacred Register**, elevated to recite the *Venerable Lord Lao’s Five Thousand Words on the Dao and Its Virtue*, and received the **Five Caverns’ Teachings**—of the **Cavern of Spirits**, the **Cavern of Mysteries**, the **Cavern of Depths**, and the **Cavern of Truth**. From the day of receipt, he must venerate the **Sacred Texts**, cultivate merit, and establish virtue, aligning himself with the **Immortal Way**, attaining longevity and saving the world, with life eternal and boundless.

Even if he does not ascend to the **Dao**, he may take refuge in the **Great Yin**, undergo alchemical refinement, and be reborn as a **True Person**, escaping the **Three Realms of Suffering**. For the **Dao is weighty, while humanity is light**—this servant’s mortal frame cannot truly embody its principles. Yet, the **Law is vast and open**, a vessel for all beings, saving both heavenly and human lives, nurturing spirits, and guiding them toward the **Mystic Extremes**. Through breathwork and meditation, he seeks the **Supreme Void**, cultivating the **Way within Life**.

Without proper adherence to the **Law**, there can be no precision, no authenticity. Yet this servant, burdened by sins across countless lifetimes—particularly the grave offenses of the past seven generations—remains ensnared by his karmic bonds, unable to conceal his transgressions. In sincerity, he dares to prostrate himself and humbly declare:

For the **Five Caverns’ Scriptures** and **Teachings** he bears—including those of the **Five Emperors**, **True Spirits**, **Jade Maidens**, **Direct Symbols**, **Direct Matters**, **Leading Immortal Secretaries**, **Supervising Marshals**, **Officials of the Sun, Moon, and Stars**, the **Five Peaks and Four Rivers**, the **Ten Directions’ True Worthies**, the **Supreme Generals of Law**, and the **Ten Thousand Chariots and Myriad Cavalry**—let them all unite in merit and report their labors, ascending to the **Mystic Metropolis**, advancing in rank to **Highest Grade Immortals**, and receiving imperial honors, with their true names duly recorded, lest they be overlooked.

May the **seven ancestral parents of this servant** be freed from suffering, ascend to the **Heavenly Realm**, and enjoy natural sustenance, while the world beneath knows great peace.

This servant’s **Daoic cultivation remains incomplete**; his reverence and practice fall short of the required rites. He has been ensnared by the **Four Departments** and held by the **Five Emperors**, guilty of myriad transgressions. He humbly beseeches forgiveness.

May the **Five-Bodied True Officials** within this servant’s body, having fulfilled their ranks and duties, return to their proper places within him, preserving his **qi** and **True Essence**, restoring him to stability as before.

With deepest gratitude to the **Most High Assembly of Worthies**.

May the **Most High Assembly of Worthies** grant mercy.

With deepest gratitude to the **Most High’s** **distinctive blessings**."*

**Chapter Four of the *Zhongliu* of the Red Pine Immortal** concluded.
**Chapter Five of the *Zhongliu* of the Red Pine Immortal**—
**The Petition for Merits to the Celestial and Terrestrial Deities**—
Having duly prepared the ritual station, I humbly report:

According to the written records, the Daoist **certain** of **certain prefecture, county, and township**, born of the **Taoist embryo**, has been graced by the **Celestial Bureau’s** bestowal of sacred talismans, both inner and outer, in an act of boundless favor.

As Your unworthy servant, my passions are unrestrained, my awareness obscured, and my sins have accumulated over years—countless and irredeemable. Yet, I rely upon the divine talismans received within my person, their protection ever-present, their grace profound. Prostrate before the Celestial Throne, I submit this petition in reverence.

Through the **Most High’s Supreme Dao**, the **Honored Lords and Ladies**, and the **Celestial Master’s Consort**, I beseech forgiveness for my myriad sins—past and present, across lifetimes—along with my past and present deeds: relieving the calamities of the common folk, healing their illnesses, responding to their urgent petitions, establishing fasting rituals, and performing meritorious acts. All my supplications and requests—whether for the **Celestial Bureau’s** officials and soldiers, the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**, or the **spirits of the land and waterways**, the **pathways of the six directions**, and the **officials of prefectures, counties, townships, villages, and neighborhoods**—who have aided the Dao and promoted its transformation—from the **first to the tenth month** of this year, I pray that those who have rendered service to the **Celestial Bureau’s** soldiers and officials may be **reported for merit**, their ranks elevated from **first to hundredth**, and from **hundredth to thousandth**, in accordance with the **Celestial Bureau’s classifications**. May they be recorded in the **Registry of Merit**, assigned stable positions, and never left in despair or resentment.

When the **Celestial, Earthly, and Water Officials** have completed their duties, may they each return to their proper stations.

Furthermore, from the **first to the twelfth month**, and for all the **lords, generals, and soldiers** I have invoked, I now declare their merits.

From the **first to the thirtieth day of each month**, and for all the **lords, generals, and soldiers** I have invoked, I now declare their merits.

From the **hour of *zi* to the hour of *hai*** for all the **lords, generals, and soldiers** I have invoked, I now declare their merits.

May all be **promoted in rank**, in accordance with the **Celestial Bureau’s classifications**, and none left in suffering or regret.

The **talismanic soldiers and officials** shall, at their appointed times, continue to guard my person as before.

I humbly pray that the **Most High’s Supreme Dao**, the **Honored Lords and Ladies**, and the **Celestial Master’s Consort** may descend their **authentic vital qi**, enveloping my body, preserving my **true vitality**, curing my lingering illnesses, strengthening my limbs, causing the **Three Corpses** to wither and the **Nine Vermin** to perish, enabling me to **cultivate the Dao and dwell in spirit**, my mind enlightened and my understanding awakened, foreknowledge granted, **longevity secured**, and **immortality attained**, so that I may **cross the mortal world as a transcendent** and witness the **Age of Great Peace**.

May my household—great and small—be spared from calamity, my lifespan extended, and the **Five Plagues** and poisons dare not approach.

By the **auspicious day of next year, month, and day**, when my wishes are fulfilled, I shall present this **petition for merits** to the assembled officials, fulfilling my pledge of sincerity.

May the **Most High’s distinct blessings** be upon my humble and unworthy self.

I now, through the **Direct Envoys of the Two Bureaus**, the **Functionary of Merit for the Orthodox Unity**, the **Left and Right Official Envoys**, the **Divinatory Clerks of Yin and Yang**, the **Clerks of the Scarlet Talismans**, and the **Mounted Couriers of the Just Wind**,—each in pairs—operating under my authority during the **Three Assemblies’ auspicious rites**, for the **deities of Heaven and Earth**, as well as the **soldiers and officials within my person**, who have together attended to the **past and present sufferings of the common folk**, I submit this **oral and written petition for merits** to the **Three Celestial Bureaus**, awaiting their edict.

Your unworthy servant, **certain**, in deepest awe and terror, prostrates, bows, and kneels twice in submission.

**Dao/Way’s merit-offering functionary rank**,

**Supplication:**

Your unworthy servants, born of vulgar times yet blessed by past merit, now behold the Great Transformation and take refuge in the Dao/Way. By Heaven’s and Earth’s nurture—nourished by the Red Spirit, fostered by the Yellow Emperor, guarded by stars, illuminated by sun and moon, sustained by the four seasons—we have received the breath of life and attained humanity. Though unworthy, we dare to crave the Dao/Way’s teachings, surrendering to the Most True. By imperial grace, we were granted the precepts, inner and outer talismans, the Three Five offices, and the Three Caverns’ Golden Scripts and Jade Tablets. Since receiving these, we have devoted years to incense, lamps, and offerings.

Yet the Dao/Way is weighty while mortals are frail—how dare we bear such sacred trust? Night and day, we tremble in dread, unable to rest. From the day we received the law, we vowed to exhaust our feeble talents: morning and evening rites, chanting, proclaiming virtue, and saving all beings. We would also cultivate the self in stillness, drawing the sun’s essence into the heart’s void, refining the *qi* of practice through nine transformations of yin and yang, alchemizing the Five and Three into elixir, soaring through the void, ascending in broad daylight.

If our practice lacks precision, if our Dao/Way is untrue, we fear our past and present lives have committed the gravest offenses. We humbly beseech the **Divine Functionary of Merit** and the **Celestial Officers of Arms**, that they guard our bodies, prolong the lives of our green-robed kin, and shield our households.

We further petition for:
- **One Marshal of Divine Protection**,
- **One Hundred and Twenty Officers of Arms**,
to bear wondrous elixirs—sweet *lingzhi* mushrooms, golden nectar, jade essence—to nourish our offspring, secure the nation’s spirit, and ensure no harm befall them.

May we, your unworthy servants, ascend as immortals, attain eternal life, and traverse the world unharmed. When we move or rest, we beg these officers and soldiers to guard us faithfully, lest we prove unworthy of your grace.

**Humbly, we implore the Most High’s discernment.**

So this year, on the third auspicious gathering of the month, it is said that merit is ascended and positions are transferred. With the first chapter of the register opened, I humbly petition the **Divine Functionary of the Three Heavens** thus:

I have removed the **Tàishān Death Register** chapter of my former transgressions and fulfilled the requisite **Lawful Rank**. I now declare: In accordance with the written records, I, your unworthy servant [of such-and-such name], in the year of [so many], belonged to the prefecture, county, and township of [so-and-so]. By virtue of my birth from the womb, my past green-robed fortune, and the favor of the **Twelve Celestial Lords of Destiny**, I am now under the protection of the **Supreme Dao**.

In compliance with the celestial ordinances, on this third auspicious gathering’s auspicious day, I have been struck from the **Tàishān Death Register**, severing all binding contracts.

I further petition the **Lord of the Granary** and the **Eight Extremes Five Qi Overseers of Destiny**, that they extend to me and my green-robed kin—both great and small—the longevity of **thirty-six thousand years**, inscribe our names in the **Jade Register of Heaven**, and weave our threads through the cosmos. From this moment onward, within three months and one day, I shall fulfill the merit of ascending and transferring ranks, my name added to the celestial hierarchy, to repay my labors and devotion, and not fail in my pledge of fidelity.

May all—your unworthy servant and my green-robed household, from eldest to youngest, from high to low—thus receive this grace, our destinies prolonged forever, as eternal descendants of Heaven.

Though I bear countless faults and sins, I beg for mercy and absolution. **Humbly, I await the Most High’s discernment.**

The **Flying Dragon Officials** and the **Left and Right Dragon-Tiger Lords**, each eighteen in number, now present me with a memorial petition in accordance with this year’s month and day, solemnly beseeching the removal of my name from the **Dead Register of Mount Tai**. I submit this memorial to the **Celestial Hall of the Most High**.

For the **memorial of the departed’s merit**, I humbly declare:
In accordance with the records, I, **[Name]**, of the year **[Year]**, reside in **[State]-[County]-[Village]-[Precinct]**. By virtue of being born of mortal flesh and blood, I have traversed a thousand-year cycle of destiny, yet in this age of the **Most High’s Enlightened Dao**, I have encountered the **Alliance of the Sacred and the Rectification of the Teachings**, driving away filth and rebellion.

Yet I, **[Name]**, am born with **obscure and dull qi**, my six senses stifled, my hundred virtues flawed, and I have no merit to offer in return to the **Great Creator**. It is said that the **Dao’s law** decrees that on auspicious days of the **Three Assemblies**, the **Most High Lord Lao**’s grace flows to the **Eight Extremes**, his blessings permeating all. Thus, both the living and the dead are enfolded in mercy.

Therefore, I now submit this memorial to the **Three Celestial Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**, the **Nine River Water Emperor**, **River Spirit**, and their attendants, beseeching them to grant me this favor: that all my **seven generations of ancestors**, both the **predeceased and those who have passed in spirit**, may be absolved of all past sins and grave offenses. May they be **pardoned and released**, granted **ritual purification**, and ascend to the **Office of Immortal Life in the Mysterious Capital**, their spirits ascending to the **Purple Enclosure**, where sustenance and raiment shall be naturally provided.

May my entire lineage thus receive the **abiding blessings**, with boundless fortune and longevity, our names inscribed in the **Jade Register’s Green Pages**, both the living and the dead secure in peace, forever as **eternal descendants of Heaven**, shining forth the **Kingly Dao’s pure and true faith**.

I await the **Most High’s discernment**.

**Memorial of Merit for the Departed** (submitted in the third month, at the appointed hour).

**Memorial of Merit for the Departed (Continued)**

Having established my **lawful station**, I humbly submit:

In accordance with the **Mysterious Teachings**, it is recorded that the **Most High’s Dao-qi** has transformed all beings born of the womb—each with their coarse and impure essence—through its boundless grace, extending to the eight extremes. By bestowing **Dao-law** and nurturing all life, I, through fortune, have returned to the **Law-gate**. The **Celestial Master**, in compassion, has granted me this office.

Yet, with my base and vulgar nature, my senses dull and unassisted, I lack the means to aid others. Night and day, I tremble in anxiety, unable to find peace.

In accordance with the **Sacred Scriptures**, the **Celestial Master’s** decrees mandate three annual assemblies of merit, particularly on the fifth day of the tenth month, when all **Meritorious Deeds** are proclaimed.

I now enumerate the **talismans** under my charge, detailing their **Dao-words** and edicts: the **common folk and cultivated beings**, male and female, noble and lowly—all registered by **command, household, age, rank, and name**, as listed below.

Since the seventh day of the seventh month of this year, I have received the **Most High’s Three Celestial Dao of the Limitless**, the **Lords and Masters of the Law**, and the **Celestial Master’s Teachings**, instructing the people, healing the sick, and aiding the nation’s fate. Even the **fleshly beings** have abandoned vice for virtue, forsaken rebellion for obedience, cast off the old for the new, and discarded falsehood for truth.

As **Functionary of the Military and Divine Officials**, **Divine Decisor of Yin-Yang**, and **Keeper of the Twelve Hundred Official Spirits**, I petition the **Heavenly Officers and Military**, the **Mars and Venus Battalions**, the **Ghostly Qi Officials**, the **Supreme Pure Lord**, the **Five Qi Scripture Lords**, the **Vermilion Bird Lord**, the **Heavenly Physicians of Sun and Moon**, the **Harmonizing Physicians**, the **Daring and Vigorous Officials of the Primordial**, the **Lords of the Hundred Creatures**, the **Divine Males and Females**, the **Mysterious Males and Females**, the **Jade Males and Females**, the **Plain Males and Females**, the **Immortal Males and Females**, and the **Deceptive Officials and Transfiguring Lords**—that they heal sickness, resolve disputes, bless travel, oversee marriages and burials, and grant protection to supplicants.

Within my jurisdiction, the **Supervisory and Summoning Officials**, the **Two Mysterious, Three Primordial, and Four Beginning Lords**, and the **Four Wilds, Five Wilds, and Seven Wilds of the Levelled Districts** oversee the **fields, silkworms, and livestock**, providing double protection.

The **Celestial Master’s** appointed **Twenty-Four Administrations**, the **Thirty-Six Pacifying Lodges**, and the **Nine Regions and Eight Extremes’ Lords and Officials**, along with the **Five Directions’ Exorcising Lords and Officials**—the **Eastern Nine Yi**, the **Southern Eight Man**, the **Western Six Rong**, the **Northern Five Di**, and the **Central Three Qin**—and the **Yellow Book Commanders of the Twelve Monthly Decrees**, both **Male and Female Officials**, the **Twenty-Four Officials**, the **Male and Female Roles**, and the **Twenty-Four Roles**, as well as the **Household Talisman Officials** under their charge, petition the **Three Generals of the Residence** and the **Twenty-Four Officials**, along with **Three Hundred Thousand Soldiers**, the **Three Ancestral Generations and Five Ancestral Generations**, and the **Five Generals and Five Spirits**—that they safeguard the **fleshly beings’ households**, ensuring all remain upright.

To the **Laboring Lords and Exhausted Officials**, I pray that all may be **proclaimed for merit and promoted**.

As my understanding of **ghostly qi** is deficient, I humbly request the **Han Southern昌 Assembly Lords** and the **Restoration of Merit Lords**, along with **One Hundred Twenty Officials**, to oversee the **ranking of all officials**. Those with merit shall be **promoted accordingly**, their **ghostly qi** examined and rectified—from the **Ten Grades up to the Hundredth**, and from the **Thousandth up to the Ten Thousandth**—ascending to the **Central Palace** in proportion to their deeds, each returning to their original station.

For those **displaying merit**, let them be assigned to the **Convenience Bureau** with stable positions, lest they lose hope. Should any harbor resentment, let them be **proclaimed for merit and promoted** by the fifth day of the first month next year.

I and the **Dao-citizens** under my charge shall **recite the names in order**, as proof of sincerity.

For my countless sins and transgressions, I beseech **forgiveness from the Most High**.

**Awaiting the Most High’s decree.**

**Memorial of Merit and Function for the Triple Assembly**

Humble Daoist of [Certain] Prefecture and County, [Name], aged [X], born in the [month] of [year], prostrates and respectfully memorializes:

To the Most High Laozi, Celestial Master, Successor Master, Lineage Master, the Three Masters and their Consorts, and the Officials of the Gate:

I, [Name], a thousandfold fortunate, have encountered the Mysterious Wind and presumptuously entered the Dao-gate. Clad in the robes of the Way, I have been graciously initiated by the Venerable Teachers, granted sacred scriptures to rectify my life, and thus ascended from the first stage of Zhengyi to the utmost realm of Shangqing.

Alas, though my nature is coarse and the Law refined, my transgressions are vast. I neglect morning and evening incense-offerings, fail to observe the New Moon and Full Moon rites, miss the Triple Assembly and Triple Meeting rituals, and violate the solemnities of the Eight Festivals and Regengshen days. My body has been impure, clashing with the Celestial Officials; my words have betrayed my thoughts, violating statutes and prohibitions. Sometimes my mind wanders, generating vain fantasies; at others, my joy and anger are untimed, my drink and food excessive.

Such crimes are boundless, without measure—day by day, month by month, with no means to purify them. Now, on the auspicious day of the Triple Assembly in the year [X], I humbly present this **Memorial of Merit and Function for the Great Law** (one copy) and the **Memorial of Merit and Function for the Mixed Five and Seven Scriptures** (one copy), along with my offerings.

I pray that the Most High Three Sages and the Celestial Masters, in their boundless mercy, extend their boundless grace, washing away my past sins and absolving my former offenses. May I also beseech that the sacred scriptures I bear—such as the *Zhengyi Dongyuan* and others, including those of Shangqing, Shangxian, Shangling, the Two Officials and Soldiers, the Celestial Children and Jade Maidens, and the Civil and Martial Attendants—all speak of my merit and labor on my behalf, advancing my rank and bestowing rewards. When the merit is received, may all return to my person, soothing the officials and guarding my body.

May calamities and disasters be dispelled, decline and peril extinguished; may slander cease, and grudges harmonize. May the talismans, ritual texts, and sacred waters take effect. May my disciples flourish, and my abode remain serene. May my comings and goings be secure, and my petitions be granted.

I await the **Mysterious Creation’s** decree and respectfully submit this memorial.

「Memorial of the Upper Court:

I fear that during their lifetime, they were among the **common folk**, consuming the **qi** of all beings, slaughtering and tormenting life—all of which are grave offenses.

I am uncertain whether the departed’s **soul** and **spirit** are now enslaved to labor under which **official** or confined in the **Twenty-Four Hells**, the **Three Rivers**, or the **Nine Rivers** [of the underworld], or whether they suffer the **Wind Knife’s punishment** [i.e., the torment of the underworld], bound in the **Three Abysses** [of suffering]. I pray for clarification.

Your servant now presents this **petition for salvation**, beseeching Your grace to grant the departed [name]’s **soul** ascension to the **Three Heavens**, their **spirit** release from the **dark domain**, and eternal freedom from suffering, wandering at ease in the **blessed halls**. May their **clothing** and **food** be provided naturally, and may they receive **heavenly joys** in the **Celestial Realm**.
