**Memorial for the Purification of Life and Death (Shengsi Jiexi Yedan Jieshe):**

**Supplication to the Most High:**

In accordance with the sacred writ, the [name] of [state/county], along with their entire household—elders and young, numbering [X]—now prostrate in homage, pledging allegiance to the **Most High**.

Fearing the **defilement and impurity** of the living residence due to recent mortality, we submit this memorial for **purification and cleansing**. Within this dwelling, the **twelve earthly branches** and the **native life-qi** of the deceased conflict with the **harmful qi** of the living, causing turmoil.

We humbly beseech Your **decree** to purify this household’s **courtyard and halls**, dispelling all **defilement and impurity**, so that the interior and exterior may radiate **clarity and brightness**. May the **divine dragons** stand guard, protecting the residents.

With unwavering devotion, we invoke the **Great Dao/Way**, praying that this memorial may **cleanse the dwelling** and **dissolve all defilement**, ensuring lasting **tranquility and safety** as we have stated.

Though unworthy, we lack understanding of **cosmic cycles and auspicious timing**, yet we accept Your command. Kneeling in submission, we present this memorial, that it may ascend to the **Celestial Tribunals**.

We further petition the **Most High** to command:
- The **Green Sovereign (Qingdi)** of the East, **Purification Lord (Jiexi Jun)**,
- The **Red Sovereign (Chidi)** of the South, **Purification Lord (Jiexi Jun)**,
- The **White Sovereign (Baidi)** of the West, **Purification Lord (Jiexi Jun)**,
- The **Black Sovereign (Heidi)** of the North, **Purification Lord (Jiexi Jun)**,
- The **Yellow Sovereign (Huangdi)** of the Center, **Purification Lord (Jiexi Jun)**,

to dispatch **one hundred twenty officials** below their rank, who shall **wash and purify the fleshly remains**, removing all **salted defilement**.

Additionally, we request the **Jade Maiden Messengers (Yunü Shizhe)**, numbering **one hundred twenty**, each bearing **true essence water (Zhenjing zhishui)** and **five-harmony incense (Wuhé xiang)**, to sprinkle and cleanse the **tortoises and spirits** of [name]’s household well, so that the **great defilement** enters the sea and the **small defilement** flows into the rivers. All **ten thousand defilements and myriad impurities** shall vanish at once.

We also petition the **One Thousand Two Hundred Celestial Flowers Maidens (Xianhua Yunü)**, along with the **Water Commanders**:
- **Green Dragon Sovereign (Qinglong Zhuanshuai)** of the East,
- **Red Dragon Sovereign (Chilong Zhuanshuai)** of the South,
- **White Dragon Sovereign (Bailong Zhuanshuai)** of the West,
- **Black Dragon Sovereign (Heilong Zhuanshuai)** of the North,
- **Yellow Dragon Sovereign (Huanglong Zhuanshuai)** of the Center,

each bearing **true essence water**, to **wash and purify the divine spirits** of [name]’s household residence—both interior and exterior—rendering them **spotless and auspicious**. We further command **Lord Lu (Lübó)**, **River Marshal (Hèbǎ)**, and all **water officials and attendants**, to relay this decree and ensure the **divine spirits and true essences** of [name]’s household are cleansed, safeguarding the residents with **beneficent protection**.

For all—elders and young, numbering [X]—we pray for **freedom from calamity and pestilence**, that the residence may remain **peaceful and secure**, and that all future paths be **unobstructed**. May the **Five Plagues** never afflict them, and may their **native life-qi** flow freely in all four directions, perpetually shielded from harm. This shall serve as a testament to Your grace.

Awaiting Your decree,
Your servant, [name], submits this memorial.

**Translation:**

**Supreme Decree as Above.**
**Memorial for Residence Pacification Ritual**

Having duly arranged the ritual formation,
We humbly submit this memorial in accordance with the written decree.
From **[State] [County] [Name]**, we now petition for grace,
With sincere devotion and prostration, our words laid bare:
Though unworthy, we have summoned misfortune through our own deeds.
Since construction began on this residence,
No pacification rites have been performed—
Lest the earthwork and labor disturb the resident deities,
And harm the household’s life-qi, lifespan, and silkworm chambers.
Daring not to act unilaterally, we now respectfully request
The **Twelve Taboos of Residence Pacification** in written form,
To safeguard the household’s well-being as listed.

With singular devotion, we invoke the **Dao**,
And through this petition, seek Your benevolent response,
That the sacred teachings may be verified and applied,
To demonstrate the efficacy of the rites before the Five Directions’ Spirits.

We further petition the **Celestial Officials** to designate
For **[Name]’s Residence** the **Twelve Taboos of the Twenty-Four Solar Terms**,
The **Great General of the Year-Pillar (Tàisuì Dàjiāngjūn)**,
The **Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, and Dark Warrior**,
The **Hidden Dragon within the residence, Sunrise and Sunset Deities**,
The household’s life-qi and lifespan, and all resident spirits—
None of whom have yet received ritual pacification.
On a chosen auspicious day, we shall solemnly install the ritual seat in the courtyard,
Lay out the sacred tokens,
And declare the residence’s **Twelve Taboos of the Twenty-Four Solar Terms**,
Dividing and resolving their prohibitions.

We now prostrate and submit this memorial in supplication to the **Celestial Tribunals**.
May the overseeing officials deign to inspect this matter.
If Your grace is granted, we shall further petition for:
- **Five Heavenly Officials** (to oversee the petition),
- **Five Residence-Construction Officials**,
- **Five Earth-Settling Officials**,
And their subordinate officers—**one hundred twenty in total**,
Along with **ten thousand generals**,
And a combined force of **twenty-four officers and thirty thousand soldiers**,
As well as the resident deities of this domain and their subordinate territorial spirits,
To jointly oversee and bind:
The **Four Directions, Eight Sides, Interior and Exterior, Twelve Taboos of the Twenty-Four Solar Terms**,
The **Earth Deities, Year-Pillar General, Dark Moon Lady (Tàiyīn Fūrén)**,
The **Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, Dark Warrior**,
The **Hidden Dragon and its Coiling**,
The **Great and Minor Years, the Two Exhaustions and Three Officials**,
The **Nine Ministers and Generals, Theft-Deities, and Lifespan Deities**,
The **Twelve Earthly Branches (Zi-Hai)**—
All spirits within and without the residence—
That they may, from this day onward, comply with the rites,
Retract their influence over the **Twelve Solar Terms’ taboos**,
And be bound to their proper stations.
We further pray for the **West, South, and North** to be secured,
That no transgressions occur.

Once construction is complete, we shall report our merits and labor,
As testament to the purification of all resident spirits,
The pacification of the residence and its halls,
The gathering of wealth and silks in abundance,
In strict accordance with the ritual teachings,
To repel calamities from all four directions,
That they may never again intrude.
With unified devotion, this shall serve as proof of efficacy.

**Awaiting Your decree,**
**Supreme Decree as Above.**

**Petition for the Opening of the Dao/Way’s Path**

With proper ritual implements and sacred positions established,
We humbly state:

In strict accordance with the written records,
[State] **X** Province, **X** County, **[Name of Petitioner]**, the entire household—elders and young alike—
Unite in heart and bow our heads in reverence,
Kneeling and supplicating for Your mercy with words.

But alas, the ancestral tomb and residence of **[Name of Deceased]** have fallen into decay and misfortune,
As spirits and ghosts encroach, bringing calamity upon themselves.
Their sins invite suffering, and they drag the departed’s name into it,
Causing **[Name of Deceased]** to perish prematurely—
At the age of **[X]** years,
In **[X] month**, on **[X] day**, at **[X] hour**,
Stricken by illness, burdened by suffering beyond remedy,
And thus they passed away.

We have followed customary rites,
Encoffining the body within the hall,
Completing all final arrangements.

Yet we cannot discern where **[Name of Deceased’s]** soul has taken refuge since their passing,
For fear that in their former life,
They may have harmed living beings,
Damaged the vital **qi** of things,
And been bound to the **Three Paths of Retribution**,
Unreleased from their torments.

We know not what merit or virtue/power to perform,
To redeem them from the netherworld’s confines.

We have heard that the **Supreme Dao/Way** has provisions for liberation and redemption,
And methods to rescue lost souls.
With reverence, we present our **ritual oath** and offerings,
To the **Five Directions’ Spirit Officials**,
And earnestly petition for the release of **[Name of Deceased’s]** soul,
That their path be opened in darkness,
Unobstructed by any hindrance.

With all beings now in harmony of heart,
We submit this request for Your approval.

Yet, as mere mortals, we lack understanding of the **cosmic qi** and its rhythms.
We beg Your benevolence to grant us mercy and relief.

We humbly petition the **Supreme Dao/Way** to dispatch the **General of the White Horse and Plain Carriage** (one person) and the **Lord of the Great Darkness** (one person), each accompanied by their **officers and attendants** (one hundred twenty persons).

We further request that **direct talismans** be sent to the **Spirit Officials of the Three Realms**—Heaven, Earth, and Water—**Lady Qing**, **Lord Shao** (of the Book of Destiny), the **Earthly Official of Two Thousand Stone**, the **Chief of the Mound** and **Mound Marshal**, the **Twelve Tomb Lords**, the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Mount Tai**, the **Nine Prisons of the Imperial Sky**, the **Northern Prison of Tianyi**, **Mount Tai of the Eastern Peak**, **Mount Heng of the Southern Peak**, **Mount Hua of the Western Peak**, the **Northern Prison of Mount Heng**, and the **Central Peak, Mount Song** (Prisons of the Earthly Realm), as well as the **Prisons of the Northern Cold Realm**, the **Prisons of the Taolian** (and all other penal abodes), the **Water Emperor of the Nine Rivers**, **River Marshal** and **River Lord**, their **subordinates and clerks**, to **release all departed souls** without fail.

We earnestly pray that the **sins and burdens** of their lifetime may be **pardoned and erased**, and that any **transgressions or faults** after death may be **cleansed according to the cosmic ordinance**. May they be **bathed in purity** and **ascend to the Hall of Blessings**, **transferred to the Pure Abode of Refreshment**, and **enter the Celestial Register’s Cavern**.

In return, we beg that all **our disciples, young and old, and household members** be **granted safety and peace**.

The **Supreme Dao/Way**’s **mercy is thus invoked**.

**River-Drawing Chapter**
With due observance of ritual rank, the petitioner humbly submits:

In strict accordance with the written records, this undersigned of [state/county/town/village], born in the year [X], month [X], on the day [X], now with my own voice declare:

Though born of flesh and blood, I am but a mortal among the myriad descendants of the Dao. By fortune beyond measure, I have received the blessings of the Great Dao from the beginning. Yet, alas, my faith has often faltered, my conduct strayed—inviting misfortune, suffering hardship, and enduring dreams that are false and visions that are ill-omened.

By divination and calculation, it is revealed that the River God’s calamity now looms, threatening decline and sickness, peril even unto ruin. I now beseech the Great Dao to intercede with Your ministers on my behalf, submitting this petition to lift the curse of my declining years and the ill-fated month, sparing me from the Three Rivers’ affliction.

As Your humble servant, I prostrate myself and present this memorial in earnest. I pray that the Three Rivers, the Four Seas, the Nine Rivers’ Water Emperor, and all divine officials may absolve me of my declining years and ill-fated month. Within the Watery Realm, wherever my name is recorded, may they grant me release, lest I be struck and confined to the penal abodes.

Furthermore, I implore the River Marshals of the Four Directions—
- The **Eastern Azure Emperor’s River Marshal**,
- The **Southern Vermilion Emperor’s River Marshal**,
- The **Western White Emperor’s River Marshal**,
- The **Northern Black Emperor’s River Marshal**,
- And the **Central Yellow Emperor’s River Marshal**—
each commanding one hundred twenty attendants to descend and act as my advocates, delivering me from the Three Rivers’ calamity.

I humbly pray that the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**, along with the **Lady of the Azure Decree**, may lift this penal curse, securing my eternal safety. May this be fulfilled as a sign of Your grace.

The mercy of the **Supreme Dao/Way** is thus invoked.

**Chapter for Safeguarding the Silk Cocoon**

I humbly present my petition with due ritual observance:

According to the written records, I now submit my earnest plea, having myself recited the words of supplication. For the accumulated years of failing to harvest the silk cocoons, I fear my offense may be grave. On this auspicious day and favorable hour of the current month, I solemnly invoke:

- The **Eastern Azure Emperor’s Silk Chamber**,
- The **Southern Vermilion Emperor’s Silk Chamber**,
- The **Western White Emperor’s Silk Chamber**,
- The **Northern Black Emperor’s Silk Chamber**,
- The **Central Yellow Emperor’s Silk Chamber**,
- The **Ancestors of the Silk Household**,
- The **Public Matrons of the Silk Household**,
- The **Descendants of the Silk Household**,
- The **Celestial Silk Chamber**,
- The **Netherworld Silk Chamber**,
- And the **Thirty-Six Silk Chambers**—

to bear witness to my day and night of sorrow and distress, yet ignorant of aid. With single-minded devotion, I rely upon the **Supreme Dao/Way**.

I now solemnly vow by the **Dharma’s sacred authority** and **divine truth of the scriptures** that I, Your humble servant, have submitted this petition to seek divine intercession.

I beseech the **Five Directions’ Silk Chamber deities** to act as substitutes for:
- Their **public matrons**,
- Their **household ancestors**,
- Their **household parents**,
- Their **household descendants**,
- And the **four mighty warriors** of left and right, east and west—

to petition the **divine lords**, that they may descend and subdue the **Silk-rearing maids** and **newlywed Silk-rearing brides** of my household. May the black cocoons grow like dragons, the white cocoons like tigers, their movements swift as the wind, their feeding resonant as rain. Let thunderous decrees shake the earth, unconstrained by taboos—only to purge filth and bring destruction to all impurities.

I now solemnly vow by the **Dharma’s sacred authority** and **divine truth of the scriptures**, and further, in the presence of this document, that I invoke the **Five Directions’ Silk-rearing maidens**.

Again, I invoke the **Five Directions’ Silk-rearing matrons**.

Again, I invoke the **Silk Lord, Master of Northern Yang**, and the **Silk Lady, Daughter of the Northern Lord**, that they may grant my household this year’s silk cocoons as desired, fostering their growth and flourishing, repelling pestilence and plagues, and causing rodents and insects to perish and vanish entirely.

I humbly pray for a harvest of ten thousand *dan* of cocoons, yielding a thousand *jin* of silk.

Knowing the **Dharma’s sacred authority** as true, and the **divine power of the scriptures** as sacred, I now prostrate myself and submit this petition in earnest, that it may reach the **Three Heavens’ Bureau**.

I humbly pray.

The **Supreme Dao’s Officials and High Ministers**—may they graciously inspect and oversee.

Should Your mercy be bestowed, I shall devote my singular heart to this cause, as a pledge of sincerity.

The grace of the **Most High** is profound.

Having received the **Divine Calculation**, I now present my case in proper order:

In accordance with the records, I, [name], have today spoken my plea in person. By nature, I am of mortal birth, yet I have long been blessed with auspicious fortune. I have long followed the **Dao**, and Your恩 (favor) has been boundless and profound.

Yet, being a common mortal, I know not the celestial cycles of *zhu* and *hou*, nor the stars of *doujian* and *jian*. Now, with the earthly branch at the hour of execution, I fear my lifespan may be cut short by fate’s cruel turn, my natal hour clashing with ill omens. The **Heavenly Net and Earthly Mesh** are drawn tight, and my calculations reveal that all nine calamities will soon encircle me. Day and night, I am wracked with dread, and my true fortune is uncertain—my fate lies in the grave.

With singular devotion, I now entrust myself to the **Dao**.

I have prepared the **Divine Tokens of Faith** and present them to the **Five Directions’ Spirit Officials**, who shall immediately report to me. I humbly petition for a **Divine Edict** to be submitted to the **Celestial Bureau**, that my life may be redeemed.

Though I am unversed in the **qi and seasons**, I shall comply with their request. I now prostrate myself and submit this petition in earnest, that it may reach the **Celestial Bureau**.

I humbly pray.

The **Most High Venerable Lord Lao**, all honored **Sages**, the **Three Teachers’ Ladies**, the **Gatekeepers of the Divine Tokens**, all **Supervisory Officials**, and the **Yin-Yang Spirit Officials and Two Scribes of the Five Directions**, showering **Great Mercy’s Grace** and extending **boundless恩 (favor)**, humbly pray for the **Longevity Lords** five, the **Life-Preserving Lords** five, the **Disaster-Dispelling Lords** five, the **Calamity-Scattering Lords** five, the **Age-Sustaining and Misfortune-Transcending Lords** five, and the **Net-Relieving and Heavenly-Redeeming Lords** five—altogether **one hundred and twenty officials**—to convene and descend for me, that they may redeem my life from the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Hell**, the **Celestial Bureau and Earthly Registry**, the **Ancient Shrines and Spirit Altars**, the **Field Deities and Martial Officials**, and the **Departments of Life and Death**.

May they investigate my body for all **crimes recorded**, my name inscribed in the **Black Ledger of Doom**, and plead for its alteration: that my **misfortunes be averted**, my **illnesses cured**, the **withered restored**, the **dead revived**, the **frail granted endurance**, and the **afflicted spared**.

Though my **years are few** and my **allotted lifespan brief**, I earnestly pray that the **Dao’s Boundless Mercy** establish the **Way of Resurrection**.

We, the petitioners, **affirm our solemn vows**, and submit this **Divine Edict** to the **Three Celestial Bureaus**, beseeching them to redeem my life, extend my years and enhance my vitality, **erase my death and elevate me to life**.

Now that this **petition has been presented**, may all my household—great and small—**suffer no further calamities or misfortunes**, forever enjoying **peace and well-being**, my dwelling **pure and tranquil**, my ancestral tomb **secure and serene**.

May the **Nine Ancestors** arrive, **wandering freely at ease**, and all beings in **unity of heart**—thus proving my **sincere faith**.

**With deepest gratitude**, I acknowledge the **Most High’s** discernment as spoken above.

「With deepest reverence, I submit a **Divine Edict for Petitioning the Star of Atonement** to extend my lifespan and enhance my vitality.

Now, I present a **Divine Edict for the Nine Ancestors’ Litigation**, in accordance with proper rites and ranks, to the **Supreme Daoist Lord of Such-and-Such Palace** for adjudication.

The petitioner, **a certain individual of [state] Province, [county] County, [village] Village**, humbly submits this **Divine Edict**, stating that my lineage has been afflicted by calamities and decline, my household burdened by illness, my actions unfavorable, and my dwelling unstable. I seek to **dissolve and exorcise the ancestral litigation** plaguing my family.

Upon reviewing their grievances, I find cause for concern: my **Seven Ancestors and Nine Generations**, both living and deceased, have committed many transgressions. The departed have already been **condemned by the Celestial Tribunals**, and my descendants have not yet been granted **redemption**. In the **netherworld’s obscurity**, they now **lament in sorrow**, suffering such litigations as:
- **Burial in water sources**,
- **Funeral rites obstructed by deities**,
- **Tombs pierced by burrowing**,
- **Coffins damaged by malevolent forces**,
- **Old tombs overlapping with new**,
- **New tombs encroaching upon the dead**,
As years and months pass, my descendants **remain unaware**, or endure **drowning by water, burning by fire**, **corruption by insects, or poison from medicines**. Even **uncles, aunts, brothers, and sisters**, or **aunts, cousins, and sisters**, may **successionally afflict** one another, bringing **misfortune and woe**.

If even one of these persists, they shall be **severely punished**—**Deng Palace’s records of guilt** will be invoked—and though they may **willingly confess**, the **Mystic Laws** will still **extend their mercy** to allow for **atonement**.

Thus, I humbly follow the **Thousand and Two Hundred Official Rituals**, as well as the **Orthodox One True Master’s** and the **Three Celestial Daoist Priests’** teachings on the **Method of the Southern Peak Purple Void Primordial Lord** to **quell diseases and banish malevolence**. I earnestly beseech the **Heavenly Champion Lord** to dispatch **Ten Million Yellow-Clad Soldiers** to **capture and annihilate** the **One Hundred Twenty Calamities** and **Strong (凶) Beasts** within my household, as well as the **Twelve Criminal Ghosts**, all of which I command to be **utterly destroyed**.

Further, I implore the **Supreme High Warehouse Lord**, with **One Million Soldiers**, to **restrain and subdue** the **Five Tomb Ghosts** who, through **wandering and lingering**, haunt my descendants, causing **calamities, misfortunes, illnesses, and endless injuries** to me. I decree their **total annihilation**.

Additionally, I call upon the **Lord of Qi and Disaster Resolution**, with **One Million Soldiers**, to **dispel and dissolve** the **inverted influences** within my household and the **Twelve Criminal Ghosts** afflicting me, along with the **One Hundred Twenty Calamities and Tribunals**, so that they may **cease their malevolent schemes** and **ward off the Six Celestial Qi’s** encroachment.

I also summon the **Great General of Beneficent Heaven**, with **One Million Soldiers**, the **Five Lords of Ten Thousand Blessings**, and **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, as well as the **Lord of Stone Tranquility**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, and the **Lord of Northern Peace**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, to **ward off and expel** the lingering **malevolent forces** in the **Mystic Origin Palace**. They must **capture and punish** all **ghostly bandits** who, through **spirits and specters**, obstruct my family—**great and small**—and ensure their **immediate decimation**, so that I may **transcend death and embrace life**, and **turn misfortune into blessing**.

Moreover, I request the **Single Lord of Stone Immortality**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, to **ward off and annihilate** the **Strong (凶) Beasts** within my household, **suppressing all specters** and preventing further harm.

I also invoke the **Five Lords of the Four Aspects**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders each**, to **dispel and dissolve** the **malevolent forces and specters** within my household, which **disturb and harass** my dwelling, causing **instability and unrest**. They must **capture and sever**, **distinguishing pure from impure**, and **resolve all litigations and tribulations**.

Furthermore, I petition the **Lord of the Red Heaven Who Devours Qi**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, to **drive away and suppress** the **litigations of distant and near kin**, as well as those of **outsiders**, and to **apprehend all malevolent, vengeful, and slanderous spirits** who **persistently harass**, refusing to retreat. All such **spectral harm** must be **severed and utterly destroyed**.

Again, I summon the **Lord of the Supreme Divine Clarity**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, to **resolve and dispel** the **evil dreams and disorientations** plaguing me, where my **soul does not remain steadfast** and my **spirit wanders unrestrained**. May I **attain peace and clarity**, and have my **deep-rooted afflictions** **cease and disperse**.

I also beseech the **Lord of the Great Mystic**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders**, to **rectify the Mystic Origin Palace**, where **malevolent influences** within my household **disrupt the spirit**, cause **illness and affliction**, and induce **fright, confusion, and disorientation**, leaving me **unaware of my surroundings**. May these **malevolent forces** be **destroyed and their harm annulled**, so that my household may **forever be free from calamity**.

Additionally, I invoke the **Five Lords of Earth’s Control**, with **One Hundred Twenty Official Commanders each**, to **subdue the Netherworld’s Palace**. They must **dispel and dissolve** the **yearly, monthly, and daily influences of the Celestial Lifespan, the Soil King, and the Tomb Star**, as well as all **encroachments and offenses** against them, so that the **high and low, elder and younger ghosts** may **no longer cause harm**. All must be **utterly annihilated**.

I also call upon the **Supreme Lord of Heaven’s Birth**, with **One Million Soldiers**, and the **Supreme Lord of the Auspicious Aspect**, with **One Million Soldiers**, to **capture and resolve** the **sequential deaths** within my household, where **malevolent influences** persistently **harass and afflict**. I decree their **total destruction**.

Lastly, I implore the **General of Auspicious Protection** and his **officers and soldiers**, bearing the **Supreme Mystic True Talisman** and **carrying the Netherworld’s Green Edict**, along with the **Earthly Officials of the Second Rank** and the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Mount Tai**, to **capture and dispel** the **ghosts of ancestral litigation** within my tombs. They must **inform the Netherworld’s officials**, the **Mound Wardens, Tomb Marshals, Lord of the Blue Forest, Lord of the Martial Abyss**, the **Left and Right Tomb Lords**, the **Netherworld’s Official of the Tomb Excavation**, the **Right Rite Officer of the Reeds**, the **elders of the locality**, and all **regional authorities**, commanding them to **sever and cut off** all **ancestral malevolence and reafflicted influences**, and to **utterly destroy** them all.

If my ancestors have already **arrived in the Netherworld**, whether they **died before or after** me, and whether they be **male or female, elder or younger**, and wherever they are **buried**, should they **encroach upon the Twelve Monthly Stars, the Celestial Lifespan, the Eight Generals, the Six Oppositions, or any tabooed or forbidden influences**, causing **unfavorable sounds, improper burial rites, or obstruction of the living’s seats**, leading to **ancestral malevolence, illness in descendants, and perpetual unrest**, then I command all such **offenses** to be **explained and reconciled**, **restored according to their origins**, and **transformed from malevolence to benevolence**, from **misfortune to blessing**. Thus, **life and death, the living and the dead**, shall **no longer be entangled or influenced**.」

I humbly petition the **Du Star Lord**, with one hundred twenty officials and soldiers, to govern the **Hua Gai Palace**; the **Zhuo Yang Lord**, with one hundred twenty officials and soldiers, to govern the **Cang Ming Palace**; and the **Tai Bai Zhong Zhen Ming Lord**, with one hundred twenty officials and soldiers, to **resolve the celestial connections** for my family’s seven generations henceforth—those who died before or after me, male or female, elder or younger—**dispelling the Twelve Hourly calamities, lingering malevolence, and untimely deaths**, ensuring all **death and suffering are extinguished** and **retaliatory qi is severed**.

Should any **residual malevolent qi** falsely assume form or shadow, **summon ghostly armies**, coerce the deceased, **injure those bound by burial taboos**, or **haunt my household**, **seizing souls and causing illness**, let them be **arrested under ghostly law** and **annihilated**.

Furthermore, I petition the **Supreme Celestial Lord of Heavenly Mystery**, with twelve thousand soldiers, to **subdue all slanderous, defamatory, and cursing qi**—whether from nobles or commoners, high or low, male or female—**forcing them into concealment**, preventing any harm.

I also petition the **Chi Sha Lord**, with one hundred twenty officials and soldiers, to govern the **Nan Chang Palace**, and **collect the Five Worms and Six Spirits**, the one hundred twenty calamities, and **wasteful ghosts** that **plague my home**, causing **loss and misfortune**. Let all such **malevolence be eradicated**.

All twenty-four petitioned lords, officials, soldiers, and clerks shall **immediately assemble below**, each performing their duties: **dissolving ancestral curses, dispelling calamities, reconciling disputes, severing retaliatory qi**, and **silencing the restless**—whether deceased ancestors, relatives, or those who died violently, were exiled, or perished without heirs—**including the eighty-one prior grievances and myriad ancestral retributions**, all **suppressed and rendered powerless**, unable to act. Should any persist in **fomenting resentment, lurking for opportunity, or exploiting weakness to incite harm**, let them be **arrested, suppressed, and utterly annihilated**, with no further influence over me.

May my **living and deceased** now exist in **separate realms**, with **fortune and misfortune distinct**. From this day forward, may my **vital essence flow harmoniously**, **celestial blessings guard me**, my **five zang and six fu regulate**, my **true essence replenish internally**, all **illnesses vanish**, my **endeavors prosper**, and **merit grow daily**, while **auspiciousness descends** and **malevolence disperses**, benefiting both **public and private spheres**. May all—living and dead—**rely upon this grace**.

The petitioned **celestial officials, soldiers, and clerks**, both civil and martial, shall **record their diligence**, **expel ghostly harm**, and **achieve merit in suppression**. I humbly request **promotion and rewards** in accordance with their ranks, as per the **Heavenly Tribunal’s standard procedures**, lest they harbor resentment.

I offer **forty bolts of purple-patterned silk**, twelve dou of rice, one thousand two hundred coins, a set of **ceremonial robes**, one hundred twenty sheets of petition paper, two catties of ink, two writing brushes, one liang of cinnabar, a writing knife, one mat, and one towel—**to recompense their labor**.

With deepest gratitude to the **Supreme Sage**.

I, **[Name]**, suffering illness, **petition to resolve the ancestral retributions** of my deceased, **presenting a Great Tomb Litigation Tablet** to the heavens.

Additionally, the **Great Tomb Litigation Tablet**, originating from the **Seven Immortals of Mao Shan**, states:

**Master Xu the Historian** said: *"To ascend, one must first resolve the grievances of the three past lives. The Western Spirit Lady instructed me to seek a Daoist official to petition this Tomb Litigation Tablet, thereby purifying ancestral debts."*

The tablet contains **ritual stipulations**. If petitioning tomorrow, tonight **prepare five bathing chambers**, as one would for purification, with **full devotion**, and **three sets of small garments**, along with silver and coins, **offered to the deceased for cleansing**.

After completing the petition tomorrow, **burn the tablet**. Alongside it, **burn the garments and coins**, ensuring all are **pure and complete**.

It is further said: *"If a family’s affairs decline, their lineage falters, and they suffer prolonged illness, misfortune, and stagnation—with descendants suffering—it is due to ancestral litigation and restless spirits **afflicting the living**. Petitioning this tablet **three times within a year** shall bring great benefit."*

Adjust the wording as needed, **keeping it concise and proper**, without redundancy.

**Ritual Position Established:**
I, **[Name]**, an official of **[Title]**, aged **[Age]**, born on the **[Day]** of **[Month]**, of **[Province]-[County]-[Village]**, with **[Name]** as household head, **now kneel and prostrate**, humbly stating:

By **birth and fortune**, I have **received the Dao’s blessings**, nurtured by its grace, and attained this life. Yet, I have **transgressed or sought improperly**—whether in **pursuing office, enduring illness, or seeking atonement**—all **recorded in this petition**.

My **deeds have strayed from virtue**, my **actions defied reason**, and though I **strive to amend**, my **merit is insufficient**. This has **invoked ancestral retribution** and **brought misfortune upon the living**, causing **ominous dreams, repeated setbacks, and lingering afflictions**. I fear **ancestral litigation persists**, with the deceased **petitioning me for resolution**.

I, **[Name]**, having investigated: **Human life draws from yin and yang’s pure qi**, received from parents, with **bloodline ties extending seven generations**, and **collateral relations to uncles and brothers**. **Virtue and vice are shared**, and **prosperity or decline follow in kind**. The **celestial bureaucracy’s rewards and punishments** extend only so far; the **Netherworld’s judgments** should not **exceed these bounds**.

The bonds of service having grown distant, the afflictions naturally abate.
Moreover, each has their own descendants, not mingling indiscriminately.
I, considering the restless spirits of the deceased—
when they move, they interact with material forms—
the records confirm this, and such cases are numerous.

Yet, the fleshly eyes are obscured and cannot perceive,
while shamans and mediums, though they glimpse them,
have not thoroughly investigated.
This is because, once form and sound separate,
their echoes and shadows fail to converge,
and their luminous apparitions still resemble the living.

However, their emotions and attachments differ—
not necessarily bound by the past—
thus giving rise to many grievances and resentments,
which swiftly become calamities and blame.

Now, if we fail to ferry them across the suffering’s threshold,
to sever this path of resentment,
then the harm will deepen, and the retribution will only intensify.
Thus, the scriptures urge with earnestness:
to prioritize their transcendence as the foundation;
to guide them with gentle persuasion,
ensuring their liberation comes first.

Yet in their lifetimes, all were guilty of more wrongs than blessings.
With offenses so numerous, they endured prolonged suffering;
with merit so scarce, they had no grounds for redemption.
This is the entanglement of accumulated karma,
a calamity that knows no end.

Now, I fear that the deceased relatives of **[Name’s] family**—
their names and forms, their natural fates in the Netherworld—
are not entirely unrestrained.
Some may be detained under punishment,
thus provoking litigation and appeals.

Moreover, spanning seven generations is a vast expanse—
later descendants are beyond reckoning.
Their virtues and vices cannot be fully discerned.
Since we cannot now ascertain their deeds,
I solemnly present this before the assembled witnesses,
laying out the full account.

I fear that **[Name’s] family**, from the seventh ancestor onward—
past and present—
may now, within the Three Officials and Nine Departments of the Netherworld,
face litigation for drowning deaths,
for burning deaths,
for wound deaths,
for strangulation deaths,
for imprisonment deaths,
for suffocation deaths,
for falls and crushings,
for trampling deaths,
for beatings and blows,
for poison deaths,
for venomous insect deaths,
for deaths in childbirth or lactation,
for starvation deaths,
for deaths by cold or frost,
for deaths by heat or thirst,
for deaths by demonic torment,
for deaths by plague or epidemic,
for deaths by sudden illness,
for deaths by cholera,
for deaths by abscesses or ulcers,
for deaths by edema, tumors, or stroke,
for deaths by a thousand maladies and a hundred diseases—
each with their own grievances.

And further, there may be litigation for deaths in old age,
for deaths in youth,
for deaths in solitude,
for deaths alone,
for deaths as widowed men,
for deaths as widowed women,
for deaths as strangers,
for deaths in borrowed homes,
for deaths unclothed,
for deaths exposed to the elements,
for deaths without coffins,
for deaths with coffins but no outer cases,
for coffins and cases rotted or broken,
for unburied corpses,
for scattered bones,
for bones gnawed by birds and beasts,
for bones burned,
for bones waterlogged,
for bones crushed by carts or horses,
for bones dug up in filth,
for improper burials,
for unburied remains,
for burials not in ancestral graves,
for burials violating taboos,
for unstable burials,
for burials misaligned in height or cardinal direction—
where ancestors, parents, spouses, concubines, nieces, nephews, grandchildren, siblings, uncles, aunts, and cousins
may all bring mutual litigation.

There may be litigation for failing to raise one’s children,
for abandoning children to slavery,
for disputes over same-surname kin,
for disputes over different-surname kin,
for having no home,
for having no descendants,
for grievances of resentment,
for grievances of blame,
for grievances of sorrow,
for sudden, unexplained deaths.

And further, in life, there may be litigation for favoritism,
for grudges,
for disputes,
for unjust killings,
for false accusations—
and after death, for disputes over posthumous titles,
for breaches of oaths,
for curses,
for punishments,
for imprisonment,
for exile,
for the twenty-four prison torments,
for entanglement in malevolent karma.

Then there are petitions for pardons,
for return to one’s family,
for substitution by another,
for restoration of lost items.

Each of these litigations has its own particulars:
For drowning deaths, they allege being submerged in the watery realm, their forms drenched.
For burning deaths, they allege their hair and skin scorched, their flesh peeled away.
For wound deaths, they allege their bodies mutilated, their wounds weeping blood.
For strangulation deaths, they allege their throats bound tight, their breath cut off.
For imprisonment deaths, they allege their chains and shackles unyielding, their freedom denied.
For suffocation deaths, they allege their chests compressed, their breath stifled.
For forced labor deaths, they allege their irons heavy upon them, their punishments cruel.
For deaths by crushing, they allege their limbs bent and broken, unable to straighten.
For battlefield deaths, they allege their heads severed from their bodies.
For falls, they allege their bones shattered.
For trampling deaths, they allege their veins knotted and bruised.
For beatings, they allege their heads split, their arms fractured.
For poison deaths, they allege their intestines ruptured.
For deaths by wild beasts, they allege their flesh devoured.
For venomous insect deaths, they allege their skin swollen and rotting.
For deaths in childbirth or lactation, they allege their bellies torn, their blood foul.
For starvation deaths, they allege their stomachs empty and exhausted.
For deaths by cold, they allege their bodies trembling in rigor, their limbs stiff.
For deaths by heat, they allege their throats parched, their breath ragged.
For deaths by demonic torment, they allege their spirits in terror, subdued by malevolent forces.
For plague deaths, they allege their bodies racked by fever and chill.
For deaths by sudden illness, they allege their pain abrupt and unbearable, their suffering unrelieved.
For cholera deaths, they allege their diets excessive, their vital forces disordered.
For abscess deaths, they allege their skin suppurating, their organs ruptured.
For deaths by edema, tumors, stroke, or wind disorders, they allege their bodies weighed down and tormented.

For deaths in old age, they allege their bones weary and spent.
For deaths in youth, they allege their lives cut short before fulfillment.
For deaths in solitude, they allege their childhood without parents.
For deaths alone, they allege their old age without heirs.
For deaths as widowed men, they allege their lack of wives.
For deaths as widowed women, they allege their lack of husbands.
For deaths as strangers, they allege their burial far from home.
For deaths in borrowed homes, they allege their burial not in their own land.
For deaths unclothed, they allege their nakedness.
For deaths exposed, they allege their lack of covering.
For deaths without coffins, they allege their bodies pressed into the earth.
For deaths without outer cases, they allege their decay exposed.
For rotted coffins, they allege their bodies unshielded.
For unburied corpses, they allege their need for interment.
For scattered bones, they allege their need for reunion.
For bones gnawed by birds and beasts, they allege their lost flesh.
For burned bones, they allege their need for restoration.
For waterlogged bones, they allege their need for elevation and drying.
For bones crushed by carts or horses, they allege their need for relocation.
For bones dug up in filth, they allege their need for cleansing and removal.
For improper burials, they allege their need for correction.
For unburied remains, they allege their need for proper burial mounds.

Burials in foreign graves, they allege the wrong earthly domain.

Violations of taboos, they allege offending the sacred positions of the spirits.

Unstable burials, they allege the disturbance of earthly *qi*.

Disputes over high and low or four-directional graves, each alleges their proper placement, yet demands further relocation.

Disputes among the six relatives and nine clans, each alleges their living kin betrayed the bonds of kinship and virtue.

Cases of nurturing children yet failing to raise them, they allege that Heaven’s nature permits endurance of suffering, yet they cannot fully mature.

Disputes with same-surname kin, they allege the absence of compassionate rites.

Disputes with different-surname kin, they allege mutual scorn and reckless transgression.

Cases of the homeless dead, they allege no proper resting place.

Cases of those without descendants, they allege the extinction of ancestral sacrifices.

Disputes from resentment, they allege their *zhìqi* not being fulfilled.

Disputes from blame and anger, they allege others encroaching upon them.

Disputes from grief, they allege excessive misfortune and wrongs.

Disputes from sudden death, they allege no chance to speak.

Again, during life, any grudges or feuds with others, each has its own disputes, all arising from lingering resentments—none can be traced or recalled—yet they summon the deceased’s descendants, and all disputes stem from the inability to endure suffering, demanding retribution from the living.

Though broadly encompassing the eighty-one disputes, their branches and leaves scatter, multiplying into myriad cases.

There are also those who, in life, committed offenses and, in death, suffer punishments—boiled in hot water, scorched by fire, cut by windblades, dissolved by lightning, burdened with stones, crushed in mountains, dredging rivers, blocking seas—such calamities, numbering countless thousands, all drag their descendants into litigation, passing blame through generations.

Further, there are hidden grudges and concealed resentments, festering sores and suppressed hatreds, which erupt in thoughts and words, spawning disputes both seen and unseen.

Some, in times when justice is not upheld, face dire straits, unable to bear their sorrow, their hearts heavy with grief and tongues bitter with curses. They utter harsh complaints, invoke Heaven and Earth, defame the luminous and sacred, revile the gods and spirits, and their grievances reach the Underworld, all becoming grounds for litigation.

Or those who, in life, committed heinous crimes, built no virtuous deeds, and violated all laws and prohibitions—all such cases are entered into the records of judgment.

A hundred years, fifty years, thirty years, twenty years, ten years, one year, one month, one day, one hour—accumulated punishments add up, and all these judgments combine. After death, the remaining punishments do not cease; they cling and accumulate, endlessly across generations.

The tormented soul, restless and anguished, grows ever harder to bear, unable to endure suffering. They implore the ghostly officials to summon their living kin, demanding they face their agonies instead.

Though the Underworld’s judgments are clear, there are still those who twist and pervert justice. Some can hear the ghosts’ pleas and issue summons, causing a family to suffer endless illnesses and calamities year after year, strange omens in dreams, dwindling wealth, with no way to avert disaster.

The petitioner humbly begs the celestial master of the dark realm to review the edicts and records, and only the urgent matter of resolving grave disputes and burial records should be addressed. The petitioner, though distant from the sacred and revered, and though the paths may have strayed and been lost, seeks to clarify the source of their suffering with utmost sincerity. They follow the rites of the thousand-two-hundred officials, and the true methods taught by the One True Person to the Southern Peak Wei Lady for healing and pacifying spirits, to request on behalf of the family:

- That the Heavenly Official Lord dispatch five officers, each with a hundred and twenty soldiers,
- And that the Left and Right Marshals of the Underworld be summoned, each with a hundred and twenty soldiers, to oversee the Great Bright Palace.

The petitioner further requests the Generals of Protection and their soldiers, along with the Heavenly Official’s true talismans, to seize and disperse all the ghosts tied to grave disputes and burial records, as well as those causing hidden harm. They shall then issue a proclamation to the family, using their original names and surnames, to:

- Confront the god of grave disputes and burial records under the jurisdiction of the Gōngmáng (勾芒) deity,
- Summon the god of grave disputes and burial records under the jurisdiction of the Zhūróng (祝融) deity,
- Invoke the god of grave disputes and burial records under the jurisdiction of the Bóshōu (薄收) deity,
- Call upon the god of grave disputes and burial records under the jurisdiction of the Xuánmíng (玄冥) deity,
- And appeal to the god of grave disputes and burial records under the jurisdiction of the Gōuchén (勾陈) deity.

「When the matters of the **Chóuzhèng** (丘丞) and **Mùbó** (墓伯), the **Dìxià èr qiānshí** (地下二千石), the **Cānglín** (苍林) and **Wǔyí** (武夷) deities, the **zuǒyòu zhǒnghòu** (左右冢侯), and the **Dìzhōng jīmù qīng** (地中司激墓卿右秩) along with the **Háolǐ** (蒿里) elders—all the deities and spirits governing these regions—are addressed, they shall sternly sever and cut off the **qi** (气) of grave disputes and the **ghosts** (鬼) tied to the burial sites of the **certain family** (某家), and resolve those that cause hidden harm.

Should the **certain family** (某家) have, from their ancestors and great-grandparents onward, any graves or burial sites that violate the **Twelve Monthly Prohibitions** (十二月建破), the **Eight Generals and Six Opposing Forces** (八将六对), or other **taboos** (禁忌), or which suffer from **improper orientation** (音向不正), **unfit burial order** (哺次不得), **misaligned graves** (左前右后), **corpses left uncovered** (伏尸), or **wrongful deaths** (刑祸) leading to endless **wastage** (虚耗), and which obstruct the prosperity of their descendants, then these offenses shall be **clarified** (解释) and **restored** (和合补复), ensuring that all shall attain **peace in life and death** (生死咸安).

Thereupon, the **Dàxiāo** (大玄) **Way** (君) is summoned, along with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to govern the **Wúqú** (无渠) **Office** (官).

Furthermore, the **Jiǔdì** (九地) **Way** (君) is summoned, with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to govern the **Màolǐ** (茂理) **Office** (宫). Upon their combined descent, they shall resolve all the **Twelve Monthly Prohibitions** (十二月建破) and **wastage** (王耗) committed by the **certain family** (某家) in their burial sites, as well as the **ghosts** (鬼) of the **Twelve Grave Disputes** (十二丘墓), ensuring all must be **extinguished** (须灭).

The **Dūxīng** (都星) **Way** (君), five in number, is summoned along with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to govern the **Cāngmíng** (仓明) **Office** (官). The **Tàibái Zhōngzhèn Míngxīng** (太白中阵明星) **Way** (君) is also summoned, with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将) and more, and upon their combined descent, they shall resolve the **certain family’s** (某家) **seven generations** (七世) of deceased and living ancestors, those who have **ascended prematurely** (前升) or **departed too soon** (后化), and the **ghostly officials and soldiers** (星宿官将) who have **wrongfully linked** (复连) with them. They shall **collect the Twelve Punishments** (十二刑祸), **halt lingering deaths** (迟留逆杀), **remove the name of death** (除落死名), and **cease killing and harmful influences** (止杀灭殃).

The **Chìtiān Shíqì** (赤天食气) **Way** (君) is summoned, with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to **drive away and repel** (驱斥) all distant and near relations, as well as **ghosts from other clans** (异姓讼) who cause harm, and to **seize all malevolent spirits** (逮诸凶恶之鬼).

The **Wúshàng Gāocāng** (无上高仓) **Way** (君) is summoned, with **100,000 soldiers** (兵士), to **collect the ghosts of the Five Graves** (五墓之鬼) and those who **cause wrongful deaths** (伤死) or **afflict the living with illness** (往来病祟生人).

The **Sìhú** (四胡) **Way** (君) is summoned, with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to **dispel ghosts of litigation** (消考讼之鬼) and **unsettled qi** (不正之气), ensuring stability for those who are not at peace.

The **Shōushén Shàngmíng** (收神上明) **Way** (君) is summoned, with **120 officials and soldiers** (官将), to **collect restless spirits** (韬转不宁), **disturbing nightmares** (恶梦错乱), and **wandering souls** (魂魄不守).

The **Tiānchāng** (天昌) **Way** (君), accompanied by **100,000 soldiers in yellow robes** (黄衣兵士), is summoned to **collect the 120 calamities** (百二十殃怪) within the **certain family** (某家), as well as **external and internal malevolent influences** (中外强), and the **ghosts of the Twelve Monthly Punishments** (十二月刑杀鬼).

The **Gàitiān Dàjiāngjūn** (盖天大将军), with **100,000 soldiers** (兵士), is summoned to **ward off lingering qi** (故气) for the **certain family** (某家), **sever ghostly connections** (断绝注鬼), **reverse death to life** (却死来生), and **turn misfortune into blessing** (却祸来福).

The **Tàibái** (太白) **Way** (君), with **a million officials and soldiers** (百万人), **government officers** (都官), and **examiners of the dead** (从事考对杀君), each having **myriad ranks** (种数), upon their combined descent, shall **protect the body and clan** (营护某身并某家), **reverse the records of death** (却死籍), **establish the name of life** (上生名), and **sever the ties of deceased ancestors** (断祖世中外亡人死注). They shall **purify the mingled qi of life and death** (清浊之气), **dispel ghosts that bring harm** (破杀尸殃之鬼), and **prevent them from lurking, pulling, or wrongfully linking** (不得伺候牵引，更相注逮). Should any **lingering qi of the dead** (下官故气) **assume false forms** (假托形影), **follow the Dao/Way of ghosts** (道从鬼兵), **coerce the deceased** (胁迫亡人), or **return to haunt the family** (还逮家门), they shall be **punished according to the Female Green Edict** (女青诏书律令), **seized, and utterly annihilated** (收治绝灭).

All **fifteen summoned Ways** (十五君), along with their **officials, soldiers, and attendants** (官将吏兵等), **pray to descend in unity** (愿一合来下), each performing their **assigned duties** (本职), to **resolve the deceased’s trials and tribulations** (解除亡人考谪), **heal all afflictions** (疗治众苦), and **alleviate all suffering** (痛恼之疾), ensuring complete **peace and tranquility** (平安). They shall **prevent disputes and litigation** (讼诉不生) and **halt all calamitous influences** (殃注绝息).

For all the **certain family’s** (某家) **deceased ancestors** (先亡) and **later deceased** (后死), including **relations of different clans** (种族异姓), **interacting relatives** (亲戚周旋), **friends, servants, and concubines** (朋友、奴婢、仆妾), those who **died violently or unjustly** (横暴枉滥), **wandering spirits** (流亡客葬), or **ghosts without descendants** (无后之鬼), who were involved in the **first 81 grave disputes** (八十一讼) or **countless calamities** (百千万种殃考注逮), they shall all **rest peacefully and cease causing harm** (潜宁休息，不得复动作为害). If any **still wish to harbor resentment** (犹欲怨望), **spy on opportunities** (觇伺间隙), or **provoke further misfortune** (构扇祸害), they shall all be **seized and permanently extinguished** (各尽收执，速令永灭，不使更兴).

After this **ritual declaration** (章御), the **certain family’s** (某家) **ancestors who have passed** (前亡后死祖世亡人) are **granted pardon** (罪蒙原赦), their **souls ascending to the Three Heavens** (魂升三天), their **graves and burial sites secured in peace** (冢墓安宁), their **grave disputes silenced** (考讼沉静), and their **blessings bestowed upon the present generation** (福被当今), **joy flowing to future descendants** (庆流后代), with **prosperous offspring** (子孙隆茂), **illustrious careers and scholarship** (宦学光显), **successful plans and endeavors** (计图胜展), and **flourishing public and private affairs** (公私利昌). Their **illnesses shall be cured** (疾病除差), **malevolent influences dispelled** (怪消), **dreams normalized** (梦正), and both the **living and the dead shall receive blessings** (存亡获福), as **proof of their efficacy** (以为效信).

The **Heavenly Officials** (天官) shall, in accordance with the **ritual declaration** (都章), **acknowledge the merits** (言功), and **not betray the solemn oath** (不负丹誓).

The **supplication** (恩唯) is made to the **Supreme Dao/Way** (太上分别).

**The humble petitioner** (求哀臣愚) **begs for mercy.**」

The humble petitioner, through the **direct envoys of the Two Officials** (二官直使), the **Chief of Rectification under the Supreme Dao/Way** (正一功曹), the **Left and Right Envoys of the Heavenly Officials** (左右官使者), the **Divine Clerks of Yin and Yang** (阴阳神次吏), the **Clerks of the Science of Vehicles and Crimson Symbols** (科车赤符吏), and the **Clerks of the Just Wind Cavalry stationed on the Way** (刚风骑置驿马上章吏), each with their respective pairs, humbly presents this **petition of supplication to the Heavenly Officials** (天官分解亡人冢墓考讼殃祟安死利生制灭祸害乞恩章) on behalf of the **officer [name] of lowly rank** (某官某乙身), who is **ensnared in official stagnation** (处官徒), with **rank and position unchanging** (官职沉滞，名位不迁), or even **declining for generations** (累代门户衰微), his **descendants suffering hardship** (子孙凌替), or **public and private affairs beset by calamity** (官私屯厄), and **slanderous tongues rising** (口舌横生). The petitioner **speaks as he wills** (任随本意言之), yet **adjusts according to circumstances** (在临时改张).

This **supplication for the Heavenly Officials to dissolve the deceased’s tomb and settle posthumous trials, curses, and calamities, ensuring peace for the dead and benefit for the living, and extinguishing all misfortunes** (天官分解亡人冢墓考讼殃祟安死利生制灭祸害乞恩章) is now **offered to the Supreme Dao/Way of [specific deity’s] Court** (太上某宫曹治).

The petitioner **humbly awaits your response** (伏须告报), **truly fearful and trembling** (臣某诚惶诚恐), **prostrates and bows twice in reverence** (稽首再拜以闻).

**End of Volume Five of the *赤松子章* (赤松子章历)**
**End of Volume Six of the *赤松子章* (赤松子章历)**
**Supplication for Bathing the Deceased** (沐浴章)

The petitioner, **having carefully reviewed the written records and right decrees** (谨按文书右牒), **today prostrates in supplication** (即日稽首), **looking upward to consider** that the deceased, in life, **accumulated many sins and transgressions** (多诸罪累), and after death, **was imprisoned within the Three Heavenly Departments** (没命之后，囚闭三官), **suffering hardship without reprieve** (困苦之中). Yet even then, **no deliverance was granted** (未蒙解脱).

Now, the petitioner **humbly relies upon the power of the Great Dao/Way** (谨凭 大道之力) to **rescue and save the wandering soul from past karmic debts and transgressions** (拯济幽魂宿业愆尤), **cleansing them thoroughly today** (以今荡涤).

The petitioner **brings forth the deceased’s garments from life** (谨赍亡人在生衣物), as well as **auspicious coins, rice, incense, oil, colored brushes, ink, and other ritual offerings** (镇信钱米香油方彩笔墨等), and **erects a bathing pavilion in the purified courtyard** (谨於净庭立作浴堂). All bathing implements are **made clean and pure** (沐浴之具，皆令清净), so that the deceased **may be freed from the netherworld** (免离幽涂).

The petitioner **now humbly prostrates on the ground, offering this petition** (伏地拜章), **to request the Heavenly Officials to bathe the Lord of the Deceased** (沐浴君吏), **the Lady of the Deceased** (沐浴夫人), and **the Thousand Two Hundred Immortal Jade Maidens** (洗浣玉女千二百人), **that they may inspect the deceased’s spirit-form** (鉴临亡人), **bathe their essence, cleanse their impurities, remove their shackles, and allow them to behold the radiant light** (沐浴身形，洗垢除秽，去离桎桔), **wandering freely and joyously** (得睹光明，逍遥快乐), **with sustenance and clothing provided naturally** (衣食自然), **never lacking in any way** (无诸乏少), **ensuring their tombs rest in peace** (安稳冢墓), and **protecting the living descendants** (佑利生人), **as proof of their efficacy** (以为效信).

**The supplication is made to the Supreme Dao/Way of the Many True Ones** (恩惟太上众真分别), **begging for mercy** (求哀).

The petitioner **now humbly offers this petition for the Heavenly Bathing of the Deceased in crimson script** (臣某谨为拜上天官沐浴朱章一通), **to be presented to the Supreme Dao/Way of [specific deity’s] Court** (上诣 太上某宫曹治).

**Thus it is written.** (云云)

**Petition for Redemption from Exile**

With due reverence, the petitioner submits this **Exile-Redemption Chapter**, presenting the proper rites and ranks, and humbly states:

In accordance with the written decree, the petitioner now prostrates in awe, fearing that the deceased, during their lifetime, often transgressed and incurred misfortunes, thus meeting an untimely end. Such suffering is beyond the comprehension of both mortals and deities. Their sins accumulated before the **Mysterious Tribunals**, their offenses exposed to the **Celestial Registry**, for in life, their **Three Actions** and **Six Senses** were bound by countless transgressions—**offending Heaven’s prohibitions**, **defying Earth’s taboos**, and **provoking resentment from both humans and spirits**. Their guilt was profound, their fate uncertain in the afterlife. Thus, with a single resolve, they turned to the **Great Dao**, entrusted their plea to this undersigned, and sought this petition, as detailed below.

The petitioner now humbly prostrates and presents this supplication:

To the **General of the White Chariot and White Horse**, with **ten thousand soldiers**, and to the **Lord of the Great Mysteries**, with **one hundred twenty officials**, to descend together and act as **guardians of the deceased’s spirit**, ensuring their eternal liberation from the **Three Realms of Suffering**, their names inscribed in the **Six Celestial Registers**, and their deliverance from grave offenses.

Further, the petitioner requests the **True Seal of the Great Mysteries**, to be conveyed to the **Heavenly, Earthly, and Water Tribunals**, along with the **Green Imperial Edict**, addressed to:
- The **Earthly Officials of Rank Two Thousand**,
- The **Mound Governors and Tomb Marshals**,
- The **Twelve Grave Deities**,
- The **Twenty-Four Prisons of Mount Tai**,
- The **Eastern Peak (Tai Shan) Underworld Prison**,
- The **Central Capital Grand Prison**,
- The **Northern Heavenly Prison of the First Celestial**,
- The **Southern Peak (Heng Shan) Underworld Prison**,
- The **Western Peak (Hua Shan) Underworld Prison**,
- The **Northern Peak (Heng Shan) Underworld Prison**,
- The **Central Peak (Song Shan) Underworld Prison**,
- The **Northern Capital Frozen Pool Prison**,
- The **Nine Rivers’ Water Emperor and River Marshal’s subordinates and clerks**—

That all may **release the deceased from torment**, ensuring their ascent to the **Hall of Blessings**, with **sustenance and clothing provided naturally**, and that they **shall not be summoned to dispute with the living**.

May the **Supreme Dao/Way** grant mercy and **extend this grace to one and all**.

**Memorial on Behalf of a Grave Illness and Great Calamity**
*(Gold-Purple Substitute Form Tablet)*

**The Petitioner humbly states:**
In strict accordance with the official documents and titles, a certain individual, born in the year [X], month [Y], day [Z], having reached the age of [W], now residing in [State]-[County]-[Village]-[Precinct], respectfully submits this Gold-Purple Substitute Form Tablet.

From childhood to this day, this petitioner has been without virtue or merit, yet has been graced with heavy honors and emoluments. As years have passed, his offenses have grown deeper. Though his duty lies in nurturing the people and his governance in soothing the customs, he has at times been swayed by private affections, favoring the near over the public, or recklessly meted out punishments, incurring the wrath of the True Sage. Even minor transgressions have led to grave consequences, and he has long feared the retribution of the Underworld, yet remained unaware.

Since [month], this petitioner has suffered calamities and illnesses beyond measure. He humbly trusts that the **Supreme Dao/Way** secretly grants reprieve—where there is sincerity, there is response—and thus dares to lay bare his plea, awaiting Your merciful inspection.

In strict observance of the rites, this petitioner presents:
- A golden effigy (*jinren*) of his form,
- Purple silk (*zǐwén*) of [X] *zhang*,
- Rice: one *shi* two *dou* (by age),
- *Zhen* coins: one thousand two hundred,
- Oil: one *dou* two *sheng*,
- Paper: one hundred twenty sheets,
- Brushes: two,
- Ink: two *qīng* (ink sticks),
- Green silk thread: one hundred twenty *zhang*,
- *Suànzi* (divination rods): one hundred twenty,
- A clean cloth: one,
as **verifiable tokens** to be offered to the **Supreme Dao/Way**, beseeching the granting of this memorial, the erasure of his name from the dead registry, and his inscription into the living ledger.

This petitioner, in accordance with the Master’s teachings and examining the celestial charts, notes that his birth was recorded in the Nine Heavens, adorned with the Five Constant Virtues (*wǔcháng*). His fate is ensnared within the Nine Palaces, entangled by the Eight Trigrams, illuminated by the Three Luminaries, and sustained by the Seven Celestial Deities. Under the canopy of Heaven and Earth, the Five *Qi* nurture his form, while Yin and Yang foster his life. His destiny is as vast as the cosmos, mirroring the laws of Heaven and Earth, inscribed in the **Central Register of the Middle Element**, overseen by the **Lord of Fate** and the **Master of Records**. The **Great Unity** verifies his years, the **Mysterious Symbols** are inscribed, and his name resides within the **Southern Palace of Nanchang**, the **Purple Orchid Chamber**, enshrined in the **Jade Ledger of Seven Treasures**. He has aligned with Heaven and Earth, drawn the breath of the Mysterious Celestial, and his fate was sealed in the Underworld—yet originally, there was no premature death. Now, however, his worldly fortune has waned: the Three Elements converge in mourning, his true *qi* ascends, and the Six Heavens resound with drumbeats. A thousand malevolent spirits and ten thousand demons harm the living, leaving justice unexalted and wrongs unredressed. The **Three Corpses** and wandering souls soar through the heavens, while vengeful ghosts wail, accusing the Three Officials. Though Heaven is high and the Underworld distant, their pleas are unheeded, and their suffering extends to the living. Even his ancestors, both internal and external, have been harmed, their essences disrupted, leading to calamity.

This petitioner, referencing the **Nine Methods of the Celestial Master** and the *Yuanchen Bao Gou Command Decisions*, knows that human life, whether born under auspicious or inauspicious stars, has a predetermined span—whether long or short, marked by years, months, days, and hours. If one is born under auspicious virtue, they shall long enjoy the Five Blessings; if they encounter punishments or harm, they shall meet the Six Extremities.

Upon investigation, this petitioner’s native star is **[X]**, his given name **[Y]**, and as a ghost, he has endured [Z] years of calamity and suffering.

It is heard that the **Supreme Dao/Way** is universally compassionate, favoring life and abhorring death, rescuing from all disasters and dissolving all calamities. Those born must live, and those who have perished must be restored. Out of pity for his family and mercy for his suffering, this petitioner, though unworthy of his official duties and charged with proclaiming benevolent governance, dares to lay bare this humble plea before the **Supreme Without-Extremity Dao/Way**, the **Supreme Venerable Lord Lao**, the **Honored Lords and Masters**, the **Celestial Master and Female Teacher**, and the **Three Teachers and All Revered Ones**, beseeching them to extend great mercy, grant a special pardon, and absolve this petitioner of his past transgressions and myriad sins. May the **Dao/Way’s vital breath** envelop him, restoring the nurturing grace of life, saving all beings, and granting him prolonged vitality, entering the realm of **Blessings and Virtue**. May the **Superior Officials of the Upper Registry** inspect his fate, dissect his years, his birth month and conception day, his past and present calamities, and harmonize all malevolent influences, thus petitioning on his behalf:

To the **Thirty-Two Heavenly Sovereigns**, the **Long-Life Marshal**, and the **Substitute Form Degree-Commissioner**, along with the **Southern Palace Marshal** and **Supervisors of Birth**—each thirty-two in number—riding **Flying Dragons and Feathered Chariots**, and the **Thirty-Two Heavenly Sovereigns**, with armies and officials numbering nine hundred million each, all converging to present this petitioner’s **golden effigy and purple silk**, ascending to the **Thirty-Two Heavens**, traversing the stars to verify his宿命 (*host-fate*), within the **Celestial Registrar’s Hall**, exchanging his name and form. Further, this petitioner requests that the **True Gods and Primordial Vital Breath** descend into his body, re-inscribing his name in the living ledger and extending his life without end.

Additionally, this petitioner requests:
- The **Five Lords of Extended Lifespan** and **One Hundred Twenty Officials**, converging to present the **golden effigy and purple silk tokens**, ascending to the **Pure Clarity Primordial Vital Breath Palace**, humbly petitioning the **Star-Degree Commissioner**, the **Name-Exchange Form Commissioner**, and the **Death-to-Life Commissioner**. Further, the **Functional Registrar Officials** and the **Great Yin Summoning and Reviewing Commissioner** shall present the **golden effigy and purple silk**, descending to the **Northern Dipper Great Yin Consort’s First Layer of the Underworld**, within the **Great Yin’s Dead Registry Vault**, exchanging this petitioner’s name and form, inscribing his living name in the **Jade Calendar of the Living Ledger**, and extending his life without limit.

Moreover, this petitioner requests:
- **[Illegible] Lords**, five in number, with one hundred twenty officials each,
- The **Five Sovereigns of Ten Thousand Blessings and Disaster Relief**, with one hundred twenty officials each,
- The **Three Heavenly Lords of Calamity Relief** and the **Five Lords of Harm Relief**, converging to dissolve the **year, month, day, and hour** of this petitioner’s birth that clash with the **Five Stars and Twenty-Eight Constellations**, as well as the **Malevolent Host** and **Evil Constellations**. May the **Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper** erase his name from the dead registry, may **Acquisition and Mars** sever his fate of death, may **Luck and Uprightness** exchange his form of death, may **Literature and Martial** remove his name from the dead records, and may the **Heavenly Ropes and Broken Army** spare him from lethal *qi*.

May the **Three High Tribunals** relieve this petitioner of the **Six Calamities** of his lifespan—**excessive punishment, disease, death, and mourning**, the calamities of **years, months, days, and hours**, the calamities of **Heaven and Earth**, of **prisons**, of **bandits and war**, and of the **Four Seasons and Five Phases (Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth)**—and may all **thousand malevolences and ten thousand calamities** be absolved and transcended.

«May I humbly petition the **Nine Mysteries of the Eastern Extremity**—the **Verdant Sovereign, Qingdi**, the **Lord of Supervising Life and Commanding Death**, the **Lord of Exchanging Names and Transforming Forms**, and the **Lord of Daoist Immortals and Transcending the World**, each one person, along with **nine million soldiers**, to ride upon **Qingyun Feathered Chariots**, traverse ten thousand leagues, and descend in unison. May they bear my **substitute golden effigy with purple markings** to the **Palace of Eternal Life**, where Qingdi wears his ceremonial insignia, and may they exchange my name and transform my form, inscribing me into the **Jade Register of Life** for endless longevity.

May I humbly petition my **native star and accompanying officials**, with **ten thousand chariots and myriad cavalry**, to safeguard my **luck and lifespan**, restrain my **Three Souls**, extinguish the **Nine Malevolent Qi**, transform my form and generate my spirit, stabilize the **palaces of my essence**, and grant me eternal life.

May I further petition my **current year star and accompanying officials**, with **ten thousand chariots and myriad cavalry**, to extend my **luck and lifespan**, restrain my **soul and spirit**, sever my death and promote my life, pacify my spirit and steady my *qi*, and eternally stabilize the **Palace of My Life**.

May the **True Sovereigns, my parents**, for me dispel the calamities of the **four cardinal and four intermediate directions’ stars and constellations** above, and scatter the misfortunes of the **eight regions of the Earth** below. May they each safeguard my **luck and lifespan**, ascend to the **Three Heavenly Tribunals**, and absolve me from the **True Officials’ summons and entanglements in the Netherworld**. May they sever my death and promote my life, transfer my name to the **Jade Register of Life**, turn calamities into blessings, and transform malevolence into auspiciousness. May they extinguish punishments with **virtue** and dispel calamities with **fortune**, ensuring that though the **Five Phases (Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth)** may clash, they also restore and regenerate. May the **Harmonious Balance of Wu and Ji** be achieved, and may the **Dao of Immortals** be fulfilled. May the **Left and Right Primordial Qi** sustain my life.

If I have offended the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**, and must return to the **Ghostly Legions**, may the **Three Heavenly Tribunals** absolve me.

May I be exempted from **hundreds of millions of trials**, **thousands of offenses and calamities**, **ten malevolences and nine calamities**, and the **three calamities and eight difficulties** of my fate. May my **lifespan be augmented**, and may my name be newly inscribed into the **Register of Life**.

May the **Bright Tribunals and Officials** search throughout the **ten directions**, and for all my **host-related crimes, accumulated sins, and declining lifespan**, may they be universally absolved within the **Three Rivers and Four Seas**, the **Nine Valleys and Eight Extremities**, the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**, the **One Hundred Twenty Courts**, the **Six Pitch Pipes and Nine Musical Notes**, the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Mount Tai**, and the **Mysterious River Northern Prison**. May they redeem my **Three Souls and Seven Spirits**, and my **Fourteen Female Spirits**. May they restore my soul and spirit to my body.
