May they dispel my **Twelve Native Taboos of the Current Year**, shatter the **restraining and binding forces of the Five Phases**, and absolve me from **major and minor assemblies, the Five Punishments and Nine Calamities, the Five Malevolences and Six Harms, and the Nine Hostile Declines**. May they harmonize the **Five Viscera** and balance the **Six Palaces**, and may all **hundreds of diseases** be eradicated.

May I further petition the **Lord of the Circulating Cauldron** to govern the **Palace of the Great Officials**, and for him to harmonize my **destiny and records**, circulate through the **Eight Extremities**, remove my name from the **Dead Register**, inscribe my living name, transcend the **One Hundred Twenty Life-Generating Qi**, and prolong my years without aging.

May I further petition the **Lord of the Southern Register** to govern the **Palace of the Listed Vaults**, with **One Hundred Twenty Officials and Generals**.

May I further petition the **Lord of the Circulating Jade** to govern the **Palace of the Earthly Geography**, clad in **Rainbow Robes and Crimson Cloth**, with a **Dan Yang headband and a Heaven-Piercing Crown**, and with **One Hundred Twenty Officials and Generals**.

May I further petition the **One Thousand Two Hundred Jade Maidens of the Circulating Cauldron**, dressed in **Rainbow Attire**, to descend in unison. May they bring me the **Qi of Contained Life**, extend my **lifespan and absolve my calamities**, summon back my **soul and spirit**, attach them to my body, record my living name, remove my name from the **Dead Register**, and pray for my **sustained life**.

May the **Jade Virgins of the Circulating Cauldron**, clad in **Rainbow Robes**, descend in unison, and may they bestow upon me the **Qi of Contained Life**, extend my **lifespan and absolve my calamities**, summon back my **soul and spirit**, attach them to my body, record my living name, remove my name from the **Dead Register**, and pray for my **sustained life**.»

The **Petition** submitted above requests the **One Thousand Two Hundred Officials, Lords, Clerks, and Soldiers** to command, in accordance with the **True Officials of the Four Wilds and Nine Wilds**, the **Lords of the Dao of the Two Mysterious and Three Primordial, Four Beginnings, and the Jia-Zi Officials**, the **Twelve Water Emperors and the River Pacifying Marquis**, and all local deities, ancestral temples, and spirits of earth and grain, to heed the **humble petitioner’s** supplication and grant that:

May my **calamities and misfortunes** be surpassed,
May my **lifespan and fate** be prolonged,
May the **Four Great Elements** bring auspiciousness,
May the **Dao’s power** uphold and sustain me,
May all beings live in peace and stability—
Thus demonstrating the **veracity of this entreaty**.

By the **Grace of the Most High**, who discerns with distinction,
I, the **unworthy**, am granted one **favorable hour**.

With utmost reverence, I now dispatch—through the **Direct Envoys of the Two Offices**, the **Functionary of the Orthodox Unity**, the **Left and Right Official Envoys**, the **Divination Clerks of Yin-Yang**, the **Clerks of the Scarlet Talisman and Red Vehicle**, the **Just-Wind Cavalry Stationed with Relay Horses**, and the **Flying Dragon Cavalry Clerks**—each in pairs, bearing this **Golden Seal Petition** for the **Great Daoist Disciple** [name], which seeks:

**Release from Illness and Misfortune, Prolongation of Life, and the Suppression of Nightmares.**

The **ritual procedures and ranks** are fully recorded.

**Translation:**

**The Petitioner’s Statement:**

With utmost reverence, I submit this memorial in accordance with the written records. Though I have been fortunate to belong to the Daoist path and preserve myself through its teachings, I have been graced with the Master’s benevolence, and my household remains upright and harmonious—yet I rejoice in this blessing.

However, as a mortal of shallow understanding, my transgressions have accumulated, and from recent years onward, I have been restless in sleep, plagued by nightmares and spectral apparitions. My waking and dreaming states are confused, and I frequently see the departed and the transformed appearing before me, causing me to tremble in great and small terror. Relying upon the **Great Dao** for treatment, I humbly petition the **Disciple** to intercede on my behalf, seeking deliverance and protection.

With reverence, I submit this memorial to the **Heavenly Exalted**, praying for the **Great Dao’s** compassion toward this mortal, that all calamities and afflictions may be dispelled.

If there be lingering **qi of the past**, the **Yearly Star**, the **Great General of Yin**, or the **Twelve Monthly Deities** presiding over fate, along with the **Eight Outer Gods** before and behind, the **Restraining Officials of the Five Punishments**, the **Hidden Dragon** within the dwelling, the **Seven Prison Clerks**, the **Delayed and Malevolent Killers**, the **Four Directions’ Wandering Spirits**, the **Hanging Corpses’ Six Calamities**, the **Twelve Lower Seductions**, and the **Guest Ghosts** lodging within—may all these malevolent forces be utterly dispersed.

I earnestly request the **Ten Thousand Spirit Lords**, five in number, with their **One Hundred Twenty Officers**, to act as my guardians, reversing death into life, turning misfortune into blessing, repelling the lingering **qi**, and dispelling the **precise malevolent influences** and **lodging ghosts**.

Further, I request the **Lord of Heavenly Prosperity**, with his **Ten Thousand Yellow-Clad Soldiers**, to subdue the **strong malevolent forces** within and beyond my household, the **Twelve Punishments**, and the **ghosts of dreams and waking**.

Again, I request the **Lord of the Sun**, one in number, with his **One Hundred Twenty Officers**, assisting the **Lan Officials**, to treat my restless sleep and terrifying specters, causing them all to vanish.

If there are **Twelve Tomb Litigants** and **strong malevolent forces** from the graves, along with all their entanglements, may they be expelled by the **Three Qi**, severing their connections so they cannot torment future generations.

Finally, I request the **Lord of the Heavenly Center, the Bold and Resolute**, with his **One Hundred Twenty Officers**, to capture and apprehend the **malevolent spirits** of my departed ancestors who linger as **Delayed and Malevolent Killers**, delivering them to the **Northern Prison of Female Verdict** for punishment.

May all my afflictions be entirely removed, allowing me to rest peacefully without further terror or nightmares.

By the **Grace of the Most High**,

「The Most High, in His distinction, grants me one chance.

For the departed souls of my household, I humbly repent and atone for their sins, seeking absolution.

With all due rites and ranks observed, I submit this petition:

In accordance with the records, I, [Name], am a descendant of one who was once of lowly official status. In the course of fate’s turning, he encountered the Great Transformation, maintaining faith and allegiance to secure his well-being. By the Grace of the Most High, he received both great and small blessings and consolations.

Yet through my own stubborn ignorance, my worship and offerings have been repeatedly deficient, thus inviting retribution.

Recently, misfortunes have plagued our household—no good fortune has come our way. My body now suffers from illness, as described above.

In deep reflection, I realize the source of these calamities: the lingering malevolent spirits of the departed.

I fear that in his lifetime, the departed [Name] committed crimes—betraying loyalty and filial piety, lacking benevolence and compassion, harboring jealousy and resentment, slandering and cursing others, invoking heavens and earth in vain, and summoning deities in vain.

Or perhaps he was greedy for wealth, stole, or acted unjustly, altering his deeds to no avail. In all ways, his actions were unvirtuous, leading to severe judgment and striking his body in the afterlife.

I fear that after his death, he may suffer harsh punishment, his spirit enduring trials before the Three Officials, compelled to labor under torment, unable to bear the suffering. His afflictions may then extend to the living, causing our household to endure continuous retribution and calamities, with no end to the torment—both in life and death—from which we cannot escape.

The fundamental truth rests upon the **Dao/Way** and the **qi** of the spirits.

Now, I enumerate all the crimes committed by the departed in his lifetime, presenting them for judgment, and offer my own possessions as pledge, to demonstrate my sincerity and redeem the countless offenses he made.

As one of lowly station and limited understanding of the **qi** of spirits, I humbly accept this burden and submit this petition, bowing to the heavens.

I earnestly pray that the **Most High Dao/Way** and the disciples under the **Heavenly Master’s** teaching may extend their compassionate and benevolent grace, examining my plea and granting me favor according to the **Most High’s** decree of first repentance. Thus, may the departed [Name]’s offenses be forgiven, and his lingering retribution be absolved and dispelled.

The **Functional Officials’** messengers shall hold me accountable for my sincerity, and I shall be summoned to the **Three Celestial Officials’** court. There, my lifetime crimes shall be reviewed, and the records of his offenses shall be expunged, erasing all charges and extinguishing the causes of his torment.

I respectfully request the **Supreme Mystic’s** true talisman and decree, commanding the **Female Verdict’s** edict, the **Two Thousand Stone Officials** beneath the earth, the **Mound Wardens** and **Tomb Marshals**, the **Twelve Tomb Litigants**, the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Tai Mountain**, the **Great Prison of Central Capital**, the **Northern Prison of Heavenly Unity**, the **Nine Equitable Prisons of the Sovereign**, the **Three Officials of Heaven and Earth and Water**, the **River Marshal** and **River Lord**, the **Assisting Spirits** and **Officials of Connections**, and all others—may they release my ancestors’ spirits, allowing them to return and reattach to their remains, freeing them from imprisonment and suffering. May they ascend to the **Three Celestial Officials’** realm of peace and harmony, severing all retribution and eradicating the records of their deaths.

If my ancestors were bound by the **Five Oaths** and **Seven Curses** in their lifetime, and their spirits remain entangled and unable to be released, I beg that all such ties be dissolved and they be set free.

From this day forward, may my household be granted stability in life and death, prosperity in our gates, and the removal of all illnesses. May this be a testament to my faith and sincerity.»

---

「With deepest gratitude, I humbly address the **Supreme Sovereign of the Highest Dao** (太上). I seek pity, beseeching:

*"In accordance with the sacred scriptures, I, [Name], was born in mortal flesh, a descendant of the officials of the Dao. Though fortunate across a thousand generations, I failed to uphold the precepts and often violated the commandments, thereby incurring retribution and punishment. Before my time, I suffered from illness, yet was not spared—on the [date], I surrendered my life to the **Three Celestial Officials** (三官). Since then, my lingering **malignant qi** (疾气) has tormented me.

I fear that my past sins and misdeeds, both in life and after death, whether recent or ancient, have entangled my spirit, binding it in torment within the **Three Celestial Officials’** domain. Unable to endure the suffering, my spirit strikes against the living. In my profound grief and sorrow, I know not how to earn **virtue/power** (功德) to redeem myself. Thus, I solemnly vow to sell my living garments and possessions to atone for my departed soul, severing its suffering and returning it to the path of salvation.

I, your humble servant, submit this prayer of supplication (求乞章奏). In the mercy of the **Supreme Dao** (大道), which cherishes the living and comforts the dead, I trust that all who turn to it—both living and deceased—find reliance. May those spirits in deepest darkness be granted ascension and liberation, as the **Dharma Wheel** (法轮) rolls forth to guide them back into the **Way** (道).

With a heart sincere and devoted, I dare not presume upon Your boundless compassion. I humbly pray that You, the **Supreme Sovereign of the Highest Dao, the Ultimate Truth** (太上无极至真), may hear my plea and grant forgiveness to my past and present self, extending Your care to me.

I earnestly request the **General of the White Horse and Sixteen Thousand Soldiers** (素车白马将军), along with his ten thousand troops, and **Lord Taixuan** (太玄君), with his hundred and twenty officers, to locate my tormented spirit and, if it lingers in the **Three Realms of Retribution** (三徒), or is recorded in the **Six Heavenly Courts** (六天), to liberate it entirely.

I further request the **Celestial Official of Great History** (大历君), with his hundred and twenty officers, to govern the **Western Water Palace** (西水宫); and the **Sacred Taixuan Talisman** (太玄真符) to inform the **Three Celestial Officials** (天地水三官), the **Lady Qing** (女青), the **Earthly Officials of Two Thousand Stone** (地下二千石), the **Mound Wardens and Tomb Lords** (丘丞墓伯), the **Twelve Grave Spirits** (十二冢神), the **Twenty-Four Prisons of Mount Tai** (泰山二十四狱), the **Great Central Prison** (中都大狱), the **Northern Prison of Heaven One** (天一北狱), the **Nine Heavenly Prisons of the Imperial Dao** (皇天九平狱), the **Eastern Mount Tai Earthly Prison** (东岳泰山地狱), the **Southern Mount Heng Earthly Prison** (南岳衡山地狱), the **Western Mount Hua Earthly Prison** (西岳华山地狱), the **Northern Mount Bu Earthly Prison** (北岳但山地狱), the **Central Mount Song Earthly Prison** (中岳嵩山地狱), the **Northern Cold Pool Prison** (北都寒池牢槛) and all others, the **Nine Rivers Water Emperor** (九江水帝), the **River Lords and River Officials** (河侯河伯), the **Assisting Spirits and Officials of Connections** (将佐掾吏), and all others—may they release my spirit, erase its crimes, remove its punishments, free it from imprisonment, and grant it a cleansing bath, robes of honor, and ascension to the **Hall of Blessings** (福堂). May it return to its original form, be reborn in the **Gate of Virtue** (善门), and sever all records of death in the **Six Heavenly Courts** (六官). May my name be inscribed in the **Celestial Register of Merit** (丹籍), and may all my afflictions be healed.

With heartfelt sincerity, I earnestly pray for Your mercy. My sins and transgressions are countless—only Your forgiveness I beg.

With deepest gratitude, I humbly address the **Supreme Sovereign of the Highest Dao** (太上).」

The **Supreme Sovereign of the Highest Dao** (太上) discerns and grants distinction.

I seek Your mercy.

**Sutra of Eradicating the Three Torments and Five Sufferings, of Releasing the Corpse from Torment, and of Attaining Peace, Renewal, and Rebirth** (灭度三涂五苦炼尸受度适意更生章) – with due reverence to the sacred scriptures:

I humbly submit: According to the written records, this lowly and unworthy servant (臣以凡愚) had meager deeds in past lives, though born into the human realm (生人道), traversing this defiled world (履於秽世). Stained by dust and impurity, I deemed myself doomed to perdition, despairing of celestial paths. Yet by Your boundless compassion (皇极哀矜), I escaped punishment and, through sheer fortune, passed the barriers to partake in the **Three Pure Ones’ True Scriptures** (三景真经).

Though I strove to discipline myself, I was ensnared by the **corpse insects** (尸虫), burdened by cravings, and transgressed precepts in every matter. Now, in the **ninth solar cycle of this present life** (今阳九运促), the reckoning has begun, and my deeds are lost while my sins are manifest—I cannot free myself. I constantly fear the sudden and unmarked end of life, though I yearn for self-renewal, yet my bonds remain unsevered, and my **merit of greenness** (善绿) has not yet arrived.

Daring to present this **remaining life of punishment** (刑余之命) at the **Three Gates of Judgment** (三掠之门), I offer my blind and sincere supplication (冒陈瞽诚), humbly beseeching Your divine truth (干杵天真), with trembling reflection.

Your servants (某等) are sincerely awestruck and fearful, prostrating in deepest contrition (顿首死罪死罪).

Your servant observes the **scriptural intent** (经旨) clearly warns against precepts, yet there is room for Your compassion (有可凭恩).

The **Scripture** (经) states: *"Unless one’s past life accumulated virtue (有善), merits across countless kalpas (累劫之功), and had their name recorded on jade tablets (名书琼简), they cannot presumptuously behold the precious scriptures."* Those who have foreseen them should all ascend in degree (皆应升度). Yet some, whose virtue and merit are insufficient, whose debts of life and death are unpaid, have not yet attained **daytime liberation** (白日飞腾). Others, having taken **corpse rebirth** (托尸解), temporarily pass through the **Great Yin** (太阴), their **soul and spirit** (魂神) enduring interrogation, lodged in the **Earthly Courts** (地官), until the **term of greenness** (绿期) concludes and they return to their former abode, ascending together in due time.

If the **Divine Intent** (灵旨) is as sincerely proclaimed, then those who follow the law still have hope (犹有可冀).

Thus, this humble servant dares to express my observations (敢申所见).

There exists in the present day a certain individual from [County] of [District] in [Province], aged [X] years, with the given name [Certain], born under the reign of [Certain Emperor], in the [month] of [year], receiving his life mandate from [Certain Heavenly Deity]. During his lifetime, he was drawn to the Dao and aspired to its teachings, seeking out Daoist master [Name], ascending the altar to take vows, and receiving the *San Jing Dong Jing* (三景洞经). He offered reverent worship, periodically observing fasts and rituals. Yet, though his body now lies in the lower realm, entangled by defilements, his virtue and merit remain unfulfilled, his roots of karmic extinction not yet severed. As the Divine Intent foretells, though his form has perished, he should be among those who attain corpse rebirth (尸解).

Fearful that, due to his uncompleted term of greenness (因绿未定) and insufficient prior merit (先功未充), he departed this life on the [month], [day], at the [hour], entering the Great Yin (托灭太阴) and his form lodged in the Earthly Courts (形寄土官). Now his coffin rests in the funeral hall, awaiting a favorable hour for relocation to the ancestral burial ground. Yet, with his virtue still insufficient, it would be premature to hasten his transfer, lest he be seen and driven by the Earthly officials (土府), finding no place of rest. His soul may scatter, his corpse unsettled, his spirit agitated by interrogations, bound again to cyclic existence (魂飞魄扬，尸形匪宁，摇动考对，注连复生).

This humble servant, in a past life bound by the term of greenness (因绿) to him as a celestial kin (忝结天亲), both dwelling in this mundane age, harbors deep concern. Though the sacred bond (灵契) is fixed, I cannot rest in peace. On the day of my appointment, my foremost duty was to guide the living toward liberation. Now, I humbly rely upon [Your Exalted Authority] to...

The **Supreme Venerable of the Non-Extreme Dao/Way, the Primordial Great Transformation, the Essence of Manifest Truth, and the Rectified Unity Sect**—with reverent fasting and prostration—now humbly presents this memorial for imperial edict.

May the **Great Compassion** take pity and forgive the sins and offenses committed by **Certain One** in past lives and during his earthly existence: all roots of the **Three Abysses** and the **Five Sufferings**, those recorded in the **Three Officials’ Nine Registries**, under the judgment of divine censors, beneath the **celestial enforcers’ hammers and rods**, bound to **Mountains of Knives and Trees of Swords**, or imprisoned in the **Nine Dark Realms of Hell**—may this memorial be granted to petition the **Three Officials**, that **Certain One’s** merits from his lifetime be credited, his **soul and spirit** liberated, and his **former body** restored.

Should **Certain One’s** spirit depart and his **vital essence** disperse, his flesh decayed and rotted, may the **Five Sovereigns and Divine Spirits** restore his **flesh and skin**, nourish his **soul and spirit**, and let the **Three Luminaries** (sun, moon, stars) sustain him with their essence, infusing him with the **Great Primordial Spring**, unblocking his **meridians and vessels**, moistening his **blood and qi**—so that those destined to **transform** may transform, those destined to **be liberated** may be liberated, and those destined to **be reborn** may be reborn.

May the **True and Upright Spirits** of **Certain One’s** ancestral **mountain and peak**, as well as the **Nine Earthly Officials** under their jurisdiction, be commanded by this talisman to provide all necessary sustenance, in strict accordance with the **Doctrine of Manifest Truth**.

Thus, his **form shall be at peace, his spirit secure**, his **vital essence undispersed**, his **guilt instantly purged**, and his **spirit restored to its original dwelling**.

May this memorial, once granted by **Your Celestial Authority**, allow **Certain One** to undergo **alchemical rebirth in his corpse**, restore his **former body**, and ascend as a **True Immortal**.

Humbly praying that the **Celestial Master’s attendants** may grant this **earnest plea**.

If this petition is approved, the **Dao/Way’s compassionate transformation** shall be boundless, and this humble servant’s **devotion shall not be in vain**.

May the **Celestial Master’s discernment** be granted.

**Supplication concluded.**

A memorial for **Certain One’s**—
**Extinguishing the Form and Spirit, Liberating from the Three Officials’ Nine Registries, Eradicating the Roots of the Three Abysses and the Five Sufferings, Opening the Nine Dark Hells, Restoring Soul and Spirit, Alchemically Rebirth in the Corpse, and Fulfilling a Renewed Life**—
is now respectfully submitted to the **Celestial Master’s Court of [Specific Palace]**.

**Memorial for [Certain One’s] Funeral and Burial**

Respectfully submitted: the **rites and arrangements** for funeral and burial.

Humbly, in accordance with the records, this **Certain One** of the **Dao/Way** has committed a grave offense—**inviting misfortune and calamity**—and thus the departed **Certain One** met their end in the year of **[specific year]**, month **[specific month]**, day **[specific day]**, at the hour **[specific time]**, by decree of the **Three Officials**. Their remains were temporarily housed within **[specific location]**, yet they have not yet been interred.

It is now decreed that on this **[specific month]**, **[specific day]**, at **[specific time]**, the **Certain One’s** coffin shall be **temporarily moved** from **[specific location]**, and their remains shall be **properly buried** at **[specific place]**.

This **Certain One** has been **entrusted to the Pure and True**, and has **surrendered sincerely to the Dao/Way’s qi**. They shall not **consult divination or seek guidance from mortal masters**, lest they be **harmed by the General of the Grand Year (太歲將軍)**, the **Twelve Monthly Deities (十二月建)**, the **Hooked Executioner (鈎刑)**, the **Retributive Officials (下官故氣)**, or the **Thousand Prohibitions and Ten Thousand Taboos (千禁万忌)**. Thus, they **prayfully submit this request to the Celestial Master**, seeking **protection from such harm**.

This **Certain One** was a **devoted Daoist**, whose ways differ from the common folk. In matters of **funeral rites and burial**, they observe **no prohibitions or taboos**. As a **single-hearted devotee**, their case is **worthy of compassion and pity**.

**Respectfully requesting** the presence of the **Five Pure and True Sovereigns (太素太始君五人)** and the **One Hundred Twenty Official Guards (官將百二十人)**, as well as **Twelve Burial Attendants (葬埋吏十二人)**. With a **sealed talisman** and the **Earthly Sovereign’s decree (女青诏书)**, let the **Two Thousand Stones of the Earth (地下二千石)**, the **Hill Wardens (丘丞)**, the **Tomb Marshals (墓伯)**, and the **Twelve Grave Lords (十二冢侯)**, along with all **prohibitive officials** encountered along the route, be **forbidden to interfere** with this household. Let **[Certain One]’s** soul and spirit **rest in peace beneath the Earth**, and may their **essence and vitality** be **securely lodged** in the **subterranean realm**. Let all **forbidden taboos and malevolent influences** be **dispelled**. Their **death and rebirth shall be unaltered**, serving as a **testimony of efficacy**.

**Upon completion of the rites, report the outcome.**

The **Enlightened Sovereign’s** decree is distinct and separate.

**A petition for mercy** is hereby submitted.

The newly departed has passed on to the **Open Way (达)**, and the **Path of Rebirth (迁)** is sought. Let the **road be cleared (开通)**, the **Earthly Afflictions (土殃) be removed**, and the **chain of calamities be severed (断绝)**. Let the **original decree (复连章)** be restored.

With the **proper ritual ranks (法位)** established, the petitioner states:

*"In accordance with the written records, this household has long been of the **Daoist laity (素)**, born of flesh and blood, and their descendants have been fortunate for a thousand generations to serve the **Great Dao (大道)**. By the **Enlightened Sovereign’s** grace, they have been spared, preserving their lives and households. Truly, this fills us with joy and gratitude.*

*"Additionally, through the **Master’s Dao (師道)** and compassionate insight, we have been granted the **Great and Lesser Heavenly Official Talismans (大小天官箓治)**. The favor is profound and boundless.*

*"Though born as fleshly beings in the **end of the age (末俗)**, we failed to diligently cultivate **virtue and merit (功德)**, repaying the **Enlightened Sovereign’s** benevolence. Our deeds were many transgressions, our sins piled high as mountains, inviting **retribution and punishment (考罚)**. As a result, our household has declined, misfortunes never ceasing.*

*"Before their passing, this household suffered from illness, yet was not pardoned. On the [deceased’s] year, month, and day, their life was claimed by the **Three Officials (三官)**. Since then, our dwelling has been restless, haunted by **ghostly qi (鬼气)**, with strange apparitions in dreams and waking, and illnesses persisting endlessly.*

*"In the aftermath of mourning, fear and dread have overwhelmed us, lest the day of our own deaths bring further calamity. Thus, we have come to inform Your Majesty and beseech a **petitionary decree (章奏)**, as listed above.*

*"The petitioner understands that life arises from the **Yin-Yang transformation (阴阳造化)**. Though we inherit the **Nine Heavenly Mandates (九天之业)**, and are formed by the **Four Great Elements (四大)**, at birth we receive their blessings, and at death we return them. The **Yin and Yang** are paired, the **male and female** follow in harmony. The **Yang** leads, the **Yin** responds, the **male** acts, the **female** follows. The **Thirty-Six Thousand Gods (三万六千神)** oversee our lineage, receiving the **light of the sun and moon (日月)**. The **Gate of the Tiger (卯)** and the **Gate of the Phoenix (酉)** mark our fate—when we live, they are gods; when we depart, they become ghosts. As a mortal nears death, their **eyes lose their luster (光堕)**, the **left side (雄)** and the **right side (雌)** are said to be the **Earthly Afflictions (土殃)**.*

*"From the first to the third day, the **left is white, the right is yellow (雄白雌黄)**; on the forty-second and seventy-fourth days, their **feathers and wings (毛羽)** fly and drift. Their **wings and legs carry poison (翅脚带毒)**, and when they move, they emit a **radiant glow (辉光)**."*

「臣以师道正一严明，生死异世，不得相干。
Though the Dao of the Master’s Lineage is upright and clear, the living and the dead belong to different realms and must not interfere with one another.

某生死气逮，注复相延，
Yet the *qi* of my life and death is ensnared, and its malevolent influence continues to spread,

如不解救，则存没莫分。
if not relieved, it will blur the distinction between life and death.

人命至重，枉槛难容。
Human life is most precious; unjust imprisonment of the soul cannot be tolerated.

臣谨为拜章一通，伏愿师道必垂哀矜。
Thus, I humbly present this memorial, earnestly hoping that the Master’s Dao will surely extend compassion and mercy.

願請仙官討氣君一人，官將百二十人，
I pray for the summoning of the **Celestial Official of Exorcising Qi (仙官討氣君)****, one, with a hundred and twenty attendants,

此时司命王耗，千禁萬忌，
and the **Commander of Fate (司命)** and the **King of Exhaustion (王耗)****, who now oversee the myriad prohibitions and taboos,

約勑四時之官，開通道理，
I beseech the **Four Seasonal Officials (四時之官)** to open the paths of Dao,

不得拘留某精爽注復生人。
so that they may not detain the vital *qi* of my soul as it returns to harm the living.

又請北辰司馬都官從事君一人，官將百二十人，
Furthermore, I pray for the **Celestial Marshal of the Northern Dipper (北辰司馬)****, one, with a hundred and twenty attendants,

收捕某死時雌雄殃殺魁綱之鬼，
to capture the **leading malevolent ghosts (雌雄殃殺魁綱之鬼)** of my death—those *Yin* and *Yang* afflictions that were my fate’s principal threads—

復注之氣，疾速去離。
and to expel the *qi* they carried with swift urgency.

某家各還本屬，
Let my family return to their proper origins,

四時之官，不得拘留，
and the Four Seasonal Officials shall not detain them;

原某前身及今生在世時千罪萬過，千愆萬咎，
I beg for absolution of all my sins and transgressions—from past lives and this present existence—

悉皆赦除。
every one of them pardoned and removed.

某盟結既解，
Now that the bonds of my fate are severed,

迁达魂神，
my soul shall ascend to safety,

去离三涂五苦，
free from the **Three Realms (三涂)** and the **Five Torments (五苦)**,

还升福堂，
and rise to the **Hall of Blessings (福堂)**,

衣食自然，
where sustenance and nourishment shall come naturally,

利佑后人，
and where I may benefit future generations.

不得更相恋慕，复连殃注，
Let no lingering attachment or renewed calamity bind me,

於今断绝，
for this bond is now forever broken.

地官卫尸，神还更生。
The **Earthly Officials (地官)** guard the corpse, while my spirit returns to rebirth.

并赐某家从今已去，大小某等疾病阴私除差，
Moreover, I pray that from this day forward, all illnesses and hidden misfortunes—great or small—

门户安稳，
shall be banished from my household,

生死受恩。
and that my family shall forever be under the blessings of life and death.

恩惟，太上分别。
May the grace of the **Supreme Dao (太上)** be bestowed.

求一及。
I humbly request the following:

新亡洒宅逐注却杀章 具法位，
The **Memorial for Expelling Posthumous Malignancy and Repelling Killing Qi (新亡洒宅逐注却杀章)****, presented in full legal form,

上言：谨按文书，
I declare: In accordance with the written records,

某素以胎生肉人，
I have always been a **fleshly being born of the womb (胎生肉人)**,

下官子孙，
the descendant of a mortal family,

运会有幸，
by fortune of fate,

得染清化，
I was once blessed by the **Pure Dao (清化)**,

常蒙恩覆，
and have long enjoyed its protection.

诚自欢慰。
Truly, I have been filled with joy and comfort.

但肉人阖门顽愚，
Yet my mortal kin are stubbornly ignorant, their entire household ensnared by folly,

施行多违，
and their actions often contravene the Dao.

招致考罚，
Thus, they have incurred punishments and censure,

顷年以来，家居轗轲，
and for years now, misfortunes have plagued my home.

丧死相系。
Deaths and funerals follow one another in unending succession.

某抱病疾，
I now suffer from a grave illness,

以某月日死亡，
and shall die on the [blank] day of the [blank] month,

恐某死亡之日，
I fear that on the day of my death,

注复生人，
the malevolent *qi* of my soul may return to harm the living,

有土殃恶气，
bringing **Earthly Afflictions (土殃)** and foul *qi*,

丧车□□雄雌之鬼，
and the **funeral chariot’s malevolent ghosts (雄雌之鬼)**—[blank]—

盘停宅内，
shall linger within my home,

伤贼不已。
inflicting harm without ceasing.

肉人惶悸，
My mortal kin are terrified,

无复心胆，
their hearts and courage shattered,

告诉向臣，
and they have reported their distress to me.

求乞请除宅中注杀，
They beg me to petition for the removal of the **Killing Qi (注杀)** within their home,

安神定气，
to settle the restless spirits and steady the *qi*,

上如所列。
as previously stated.

臣按人死之日，
I, the petitioner, declare that on the day of death,

魂魄流散，
the soul and *qi* scatter,

化成八杀，
transforming into the **Eight Killing Qi (八杀)**,

雌雄咎注，
with malevolent *Yin* and *Yang* influences binding them.

丧车□□，
The **funeral chariot’s [blank]**—

或出或上，
whether they emerge or ascend—

还重杀害，
shall return to wreak fresh havoc,

缠绵宅内，
lingering within the household,

伺候衰缺，
waiting for weakness to strike,

复欲中伤，
and once more inflict suffering,

注害生人。
upon the living.

谨为伏地拜章一通上闻，
Thus, I humbly kneel and submit this memorial to the heavens,

特从大道回神降福，
seeking through the **Great Dao (大道)** to recall my spirit and bestow blessings,

流清荡浊。
to purify the foul and clear the turbid.

谨请天中敢健吏兵千二百人，
I pray for the summoning of **Twelve Hundred Heavenly Brave Officers (天中敢健吏兵千二百人)**,

又请逐注鬼禽奇君、水坦吏各一，
and one each of the **Ghost-Hound Official (逐注鬼禽奇君)** and the **Water-Repelling Officer (水坦吏)**,

合来下某家宅舍之中，
to descend together into my family’s residence,

收捕□尸注鬼，
and capture the **[blank] Ghosts of Posthumous Malignancy (□尸注鬼)**—

雌雄客杀，
the *Yin* and *Yang* **Guest-Killing Qi (客杀)**—

丧车□□，
and the **funeral chariot’s [blank]**—

一切绝灭。
so that they may all be utterly annihilated.

一合下到某家宅中，
all twelve to descend together into my family’s residence,

收却百二十殃杀之鬼，
and capture a hundred and twenty **Ghosts of Affliction and Killing (殃杀之鬼)**,

二十四吏，
along with the **Twenty-Four Attendants (二十四吏)**,

各坚兵刃外向，

绕宅三重。
surrounding the home in three concentric layers.

云行万里，
and with divine swiftness traverse ten thousand leagues,

清严宅内，

荡除尸秽，

众官备卫，

神明镇守，

保护人口，

so that no further **Killing Qi (注)** may take root.

生死所犯，

恩惟 太上分别。」
May the grace of the **Supreme Dao (太上)** be forever bestowed.»

I humbly petition for mercy.
**Memorial of Accepting an Official Post**

With due rank and position, I respectfully state:
By examining the official records, I, [Name], as a lowly official, was born in ignorance yet fortunate to encounter this era of prosperity. Grateful for the heavens’ and earth’s benevolent light, I have been granted a place among the common folk.

In my former service under [Name]’s court, upon fulfilling my duties, I was promoted to the post of [Name]. The royal command having been issued, I dare not delay. On the appointed day when I received the seal and tablet, I bowed in reverence to the Dao’s pure and refined *qi*, and without regard for the times or rulers, I turned to my teacher’s Way and now submit this memorial to seek mercy.

I humbly present this petition to the throne, requesting:
One **Juzhuque Lord (朱雀君)**, with one hundred twenty officers, to oversee the **Luo Ping Palace (洛平宫)**, ensuring harmony among the people and joy among guests—so that all may feast with laughter and no grievance remains.

Further, I request:
One **Lord of Ranked Officials (位官受爵君)**, with one hundred twenty officers each,
And one **Lord of the Four Quarters’ Barbarians (四方夷蛮戎狄君)**, with one hundred twenty officers each—all to be summoned together to guard me.

After receiving the seal and tablet, may all malevolent *qi* of calamity and harm be dispelled, so that my career may flourish, my official tenure be prosperous, and my life secure and unburdened—thus fulfilling my pledge.

The officials I have requested shall be recorded by the **Central Palace (中宫)**, and I pray that no resentment may arise.

May the grace of the **Supreme Dao (太上)** be forever bestowed.

I humbly request one **Celestial Official of the Hour (辰)**.

In the **Edict of Governing Officials and Attending to the People (临官莅民章)**, I submit my petition with proper rank and protocol:

*"I, [Name], a man of low wisdom, have been mistakenly favored by Your Great Grace, selected by the times, and appointed as Magistrate of [Chu] County. Having received the royal command, I must now govern the people and affairs of the realm.

Yet, in these times of deceit and corruption, where human and ghostly forces vie for power, and mortal efforts are insufficient to avert calamities, I now, on the [specific] day of this month, set forth on my journey. I shall arrive at my post on the [specific] day of the [specific] month, relying solely on the **Dao-qi (道气)**. I dare not consult omens or inquire of auspicious times.

Upon entering my jurisdiction, I fear being harmed by the **land’s spirits and deities (土地精灵)**, the **ritual masters and ancestral shrines (符师社庙)**, lingering **qi of past feasts (饮食故气)**, the **General of the Year-Pillar (太岁将军)**, the **taboos along the Dao (道上禁诃)**, the **Five Phases’ Celestial Lords and their correspondences (五行王相)**, and the **forbidden omens of the *Kui* and *Gang* (魁纲诸忌)**. I therefore declare my arrival in advance and beseech protection.

With utmost reverence, I submit this petition, praying that the **Central Palace (上官)** may instruct the **local land deities (土地真官)**, the **postal couriers and relay stations (邮书驿骑)**, and the **watchtowers and villages (亭传里邑)** to clear the way and guard my person.

I further request:
One **Lord of Prosperity and Decline (昌落君)**, with one hundred twenty officers,
And one **General of Auspicious Protection (佑护将军)**, one **Lord of Ten Thousand Blessings (万福丈人)**, with their officers, to dispel all calamities.

One **Lord of Release and Exemption (解除禁害君)**, with one hundred twenty officers, along with the officials of the **Four Quarters’ Barbarians (四方夷蛮戎狄君)**, all assembled together below, to jointly guard my person, the **General of the Year-Pillar (太岁将军)**, the **Four Seasonal Celestial Depleters (四时王耗)**, and the **myriad prohibitions and omens (千禁万忌)**—so that my arrival and entry into office may be secure, my tenure free of strife, my speech unobstructed, my health serene, my career ascending, and my year’s end fulfilled with my wishes.

May the **times’ officials and officers** record my merits and report my labors.

May the grace of the **Supreme Dao (太上)** be forever bestowed."

I humbly petition for a single auspicious hour.

**Memorial for the Elimination of Obstructive Calamities**
*(Submitted in proper rank and form)*

I respectfully report: According to the official records, I have encountered this fateful juncture, granted the honor of serving in Qinghua, bearing the insignia of celestial officials, and receiving imperial favor in all my comings and goings. Truly, this fills me with profound gratitude and relief.

From my ancestral lineage to the present, my family has inherited official rank and titles, all through the sovereign’s boundless grace. Now, I am unworthy of holding this office, and on this day, I reverently accept the royal command, relying entirely upon the Great Dao. Without divination or inquiry, without selecting a propitious day or hour, I proceed with a sincere heart.

Since assuming this post, I have been plagued by unsettling dreams and waking visions, alternating with recurring illnesses and strange, inexplicable phenomena—unclear in their origin. Upon consulting the annual almanac and the celestial cycles of the Six Jia, I find that on the day I received my commission, my natal branch was Five Li, while my current year-branch was Jiawu, clashing with Zi. Moreover, I accepted the commission in the eleventh month—a month of decline. The Year-Pillar is [omitted], with [omitted] as the official killer and [omitted] as the grave killer, and I myself am the official killer, all converging in mutual assault.

The day’s influence descends upon the Six Harmonies, further compounded by the Six Calamities. I have heard that...

「The Dao/Way knows no prohibitions or taboos; without sincerity and devotion, it cannot be attained. To avert calamities and repel misfortunes, they have come to inform me, seeking official documents. I humbly submit this request, hoping that the Way’s *qi* may flow downward.

I respectfully petition the Heavenly Hall Lord, requesting a hundred and twenty officials, to govern the An Yang Palace, overseeing the removal of the Nine Heavenly Prohibitions. The one receiving the commission shall eliminate [them]. I further request the Heavenly King and his Thousand Two Hundred Immortal Maidens, clad in green robes, to collect the ten thousand people of the world, bestowing upon them titles and seals of gold and silver, granting them divine understanding, averting calamities and repelling misfortunes, and ensuring their lives span a hundred years. If, on the day I receive my appointment, the time should be Five Li, any malevolent spirits and myriad harms shall all be eliminated. I beg the High Official to dispatch the requested personnel accordingly.

Within my jurisdiction, there are so many officials—two hundred and forty in total. If it be a prefecture, there are twenty-four officials. If a commandery, eighteen officials. If a county, seven officials. All united in strength, they shall help me avert and repel evil, eliminate prohibitions, and ensure no other matters arise in office. Discussions and judgments shall be in harmony with virtue, officials and commoners alike shall rejoice, and thus I may be promoted in time, ending the year in stability.

On the day my wishes are fulfilled, the petitioned Heavenly Officials shall speak of my merits and labor, not betraying their trust in me. The favor is bestowed by the Supreme Sovereign.

I beg for mercy. Request for Promotion to High Office

With proper rank, I submit: In accordance with the official documents, I have always been one born from the womb of flesh, with descendants of mere bones. Formerly, through the *Lèhuà* ritual, I was entrusted with the Way to preserve and govern myself. The grace bestowed upon me has been profound and generous, filling me with joy and comfort.

Descended from a noble lineage, my family has long held officialdom as its profession. I have accumulated ranks as various officials, managing royal affairs with distinction, my name and reputation both flourishing. Now I return to this post, which is not something a mere mortal can achieve. I am deeply moved by the Way’s vast protection and care.

My current office holds the critical affairs of state, or perhaps lies beyond the frontiers, as the case may be. My duties encompass the grand governance of all under Heaven, where both officials and ministers are powerful, and the commoners, accustomed to their privileges, are all too familiar with deceit. There are many lawsuits, and justice is hard to discern. I fear that if my words or actions falter, I may incur blame and censure, and thus I humbly rely on the Way’s broad acceptance and supplication, seeking these officials to safeguard and protect me.

Though unworthy, I bear great responsibility and cannot bear the burden of the mortals’ petitions. I dare to violate the solemnity of the court, humbly presenting this memorial, and hope for Your compassionate grace and protection.

I earnestly request the Twelve Lords of the Nine Barbarians, Eight Man, Six Rong, and Five Di—each twelve in number—along with their officials, soldiers, and attendants, to encircle my residence, standing guard at my sides.

I further petition the Five Lords of Ten Thousand Blessings, each with a hundred and twenty officials, to dispel lingering malevolent *qi* and vengeful spirits, to curse those who seek to harm me, and to repel death and bring life, to repel misfortune and bring blessings.

I further petition the Five Lords of Great Stars, each with a hundred and twenty officials, to govern the Stone Immortal Palace, and to suppress the slanderous tongues of the commoners, so that false accusations cannot take root, and to restore them to their proper places, ensuring that commoners and officials alike meet with smiles and joy.

I further petition the Lords of Auxiliary Generals and Ten Thousand Blessings, each with a hundred and twenty officials, to guard my person.

I further petition the Lord of Azure Darkness, with a hundred and twenty officials, to govern the Great Gate Palace, suppressing the resentment, complaints, and malevolent *qi* of the office, preventing them from reaching me.

I hope that when the Heavenly Officials arrive, their single attendant shall gather with the officials and commoners of my state, commandery, county, village, and hamlet, each following their respective lord, to surround and protect my person. They shall dispel evil spirits, pestilence, and epidemic *qi*, and any schemes of enticement and harm shall all be eliminated, allowing my heart to open and my mind to clear. I shall comprehend the wisdom of the Five Spirits, fully understand what is spoken, and act accordingly. My words shall be as trustworthy as those of a thousand mouths, my intentions as sincere as the deepest vows. My household shall be ever peaceful, and by year’s end, I shall achieve prosperity, benefiting both the public and private spheres, as proof of my devotion.

On that day, I shall speak of the merits of the Heavenly Officials, requesting their promotion, to repay their labor and suffering. I beg for forgiveness of all my great and small faults, my myriad sins. The favor is bestowed by the Supreme Sovereign.

I further beg for mercy.」

The Most High and All-Venerable Celestial Worthies, distinguished by their ranks:

The **Steward of Martial Campaigns** presents his humble petition. In strict accordance with the official records, I, [Name], by birth a mortal of flesh and blood, a descendant of lowly officials, through the fortune of fate and the grace of the Great Transformation, have received the benevolent coverage of Heaven’s favor, truly filling me with joy and gratitude.

Yet, due to my own stubborn ignorance and accumulated sins—mountains high—disasters and calamities have continually befallen me.

Now, the journey is long and arduous, traversing rivers and mountains, passing through Huai and Si, advancing toward the enemy’s strongholds. In the midst of white blades and poisoned steel, the clash of arms is fierce, and both civil and martial authorities press down upon me. The military laws are severe, execution swift, and those who wield power cruelly oppress others, forcing them into violence. My merits are meager, and I cannot avert misfortune.

Fearful that I may perish in this dire strait without escape, I rely upon the **Dao-qi** of the myriad people, humbly presenting this memorial to the **Treaty-Officer**, beseeching protection.

With deepest reverence, I prostrate myself and submit this petition, appealing to the **Nine Lords of the Eastern Barbarians**, the **Eight Lords of the Southern Snares**, the **Six Lords of the Western Steppe**, and the **Five Lords of the Northern Di**, twelve each in number. I further implore the **Thousand-Li Lord**, the **Ten-Thousand-Li General**, and the **General of Auspicious Protection**, that they may jointly guard and shield me, following and covering me wherever I may be, ensuring my constant safety.

May they repel all calamities—epidemics, malevolent spirits, and bandits—that I may escape the blades of war, transcend this peril, and find favor within the ranks, free from blame or censure, as proof of my sincerity.

I shall then speak of my merits before the **Temporal Lords and officials**, repaying their labor and toil.

The grace is granted by the Most High and All-Venerable Celestial Worthies.

I further beg for mercy.

**Chapter of the Vermilion Pine Child**, Volume Six, concludes.
